## 146 - **To the Labyrinth with Michelle**

Early in the morning, half awake and half asleep, the smell of breakfast wafting through the air makes me hungry, and I gradually wake up. Ah, that’s right, I’m staying at Michelle’s house. Thank you for all the hard work so early in the morning.

Last night, I used healing magic to the limit to treat Michelle’s peach poison. Thanks to my automatic recovery skill, my magical energy has completely restored, but due to the side effects of the skill, I’m extremely hungry. As I, still half awake and half asleep, am wondering if I should get up soon, a sound that makes me uncomfortable echoes through the air.

*Bam, bam, bam* The sound of the front door of the house getting violently banged. What the hell, so noisy. I quickly get up and open the front door before Michelle, who is cooking, can come out.

「The hell is your deal, you bastard! So early in the morning!」

When I open the door in a slightly pissed manner, there’s a thug-like man standing there. When I appraise him, I find that he’s a level 11 warrior. Who is this guy?

「Huh? You bastard, who the hell are you?」

Huh, why is he being so aggressive? Could he be Michelle’s parent or relative, by any chance?

Michelle shows up from behind me in a panic and greets him.

「Hey, Michelle, where did you go last night? You promised to give me 80% of your earnings, didn’t you?!」

Huh?! Are you serious? Is this guy someone who collects protection money from prostitutes? Still, taking 80% of their earnings, talk about a predatory business.

「I, I’m Sorry. Umm, I’ve contracted peach poison, so I can’t do business anymore.」

「Peach poison, you say? Tch, you too, huh. You’re not lying, are you?」

「Yes, as you can see.」

Michelle pulls up her outer garment and shows the man the affected area. As expected, it seems like my healing magic couldn’t heal it. However, from the look of it, I think it’s considerably better than yesterday. It’s hard to tell how long it will take to cure it, but I should be able to fully cure it eventually.

「Hmm? What, it’s still only in the early stages, isn’t it? You should be able to do business for another year. Be sure to stand on the street again starting today, okay?」

「Huh?! The hell are you talking about? Are you trying to spread a sexually transmitted disease?」

「Like I said, who the hell are you? Listen, kid. Prostitutes aren’t a business that lasts long anyway. So you have to make money while you still can.」

「Look, prostitutes are an important product for you guys, no? And if customers are satisfied, they will become regulars, and you will be able to make money for a long time. What you’re trying to do is a foolish act that will reduce your products and customers…」

「Shut it, I’m being pressured by my superiors here. I’ll have her do business no matter what.」

Are you serious? It looks like this guy is so stupid that he doesn’t even understand the basics or principles of business. The same is probably true for his superiors. Are there nothing but people like this in the slums? Their way of thinking is just like that of a poor person. Rather than long-term investment or prosperity, they only care about how much they can earn that day. That’s probably exactly why he’s serving as a bottom-tier minion in the slums. Our sense of values ​​are so different that there’s no point in talking to this kind of guy anymore.

「At any rate, Michelle won’t stand on the streets anymore. She’s going to work as an adventurer with me, after all.」

「Huh?! As if a little girl like her will be able to work as an adventurer.」

「I’m going to have her dismantle monsters, carry luggage, and do other odd jobs. If you understand, get out of here already.」

「What did you just say, you bastard?!… Hii!」

Not only am I hungry, this guy is such a pain, so I use my intimidation skill on him, and then his face turns white. It seems that this guy can only carry himself in an overbearing manner in front of prostitutes, who can never put up resistance, so he gets so scared that he backs away.

「J, just you wait.」

「Don’t come here ever again.」

The man runs off. Now then, let’s have breakfast.

As the three of us sit down at the table and start eating, Cordis speaks up.

「Hey, big brother, is big sister going to be an adventurer?」

「No, I don’t think it’s possible for Michelle. However, she was granted the job of magician. It’d be a good idea to put that job into use. What do you say, Michelle, want to try working as a leech’s assistant in another town?」

「Huh, a leech… That’s, I have no confidence that I’ll be able to do it, though.」

「Don’t worry. I’ll teach you. And I do have connections, after all.」

I have connections with the trading company in the Lambert territory that Lorraine married into, and with Aiza, a leech in the Neurath territory. If I help her raise her level in the labyrinth and raise her proficiency levels in magical energy manipulation and other skills, she should be able to handle it fairly well. It’s definitely better than staying in a slum full of shitty people like this.

「Besides, if you can learn a trade and work under a leech, you should be able to live a stable life. You’ll also be able to make Cody’s life easier, you know?」

「Making Cody’s life easier… In that case, I’d like to give it a try. Sei-san, please.」

「Yeah, but it’s not going to be an easy path. First, we’ll go into the labyrinth to raise your level.」

「Y, yes. I understand.」

「Huh, you’re going into the labyrinth?! I want to go too.」

「Not now. As expected, I won’t be able to take care of the two of you at the same time. But if you do your best in your sword practice, and I judge that you’ve become strong enough, I’ll take you with us.」

「Yay, that’s a promise, okay, big brother?」

After finishing our breakfast, I take Michelle to go shopping. First thing first, we have to prepare to go into the labyrinth. Besides, I was so hungry that the breakfast wasn’t enough at all. Oops, before that.

「Cody, Michelle and I will be back before sunset. Once you get used to the short wooden sword, give this one a try, too.」

I hand him a wooden sword that hasn’t been cut. I thought that as expected it would be too heavy for 13-year-old Cordis, but he’ll come of age next year. I can’t spoil him too much.

「Yes, thank you, big brother.」

「Alright, Michelle, let’s go.」

「Yes.」

We go to town and buy three loaves of bread, vegetables, and also fruit. I do need some to fill my stomach, but Cordis is in his growth period, so he needs nutrition.

Then we go to the armor shop. I gave Michelle an iron shield, but it was so heavy that she couldn’t carry it. As we have no other choice, we buy a wooden shield and a leather hat to protect her head at the armor shop. There’s probably a huge difference between whether you have them or not. I guess that’s about it.

「Um, Sei-san. This and everything else, we’ve truly been in your care, thank you very much.」

「Yeah, I’ll be taking my reward later, after all.」

「Yes.」

Even though she’s from the slums, she knows manners well, how admirable. Let’s try asking her a bit about her life history later. Privacy can eat shit. I’ll give them enough support to offset the fact I pry into their private life.

After completing our preparations, we finally head to the labyrinth. It seems that adventurers are starting to get into work around this time of day, so it’s quite crowded. Many of them have sharp eyes. Maybe it’s because the labyrinth is on the edge of the slums, but I get the impression that there are a lot of rough-looking people here. All of them are staring at Michelle. It’s like a jewel in a dunghill. As expected, I think Michelle is quite cute. Truthfully speaking, she’s not the kind of woman you can embrace on such a dirty street for a small amount of money.

Finally, we set foot into the labyrinth. What should I do? Should I make a map? This, too, is a habit of mine, and it’s better than wandering around aimlessly. I take out paper and a brush from my storage and start making a map. I start walking while keeping my presence detection skill in my mind.

Sigh, already? Someone is tailing us. How annoying, of all things, they must be planning to rape Michelle. For them to entertain such a thought so early in the morning, what energetic guys. Well, no matter how you look at it, Michelle, wearing an awkward leather helmet and holding a wooden shield nervously, is a delicate girl who looks unsuited to be here. She’s probably the perfect prey for ill-intended people. Although I’m not wearing my demonic dragon armor, I’m still pretty well-dressed, so perhaps they’re planning to rob me. Well, I guess both.

What should I do? I don’t mind turning them into Michelle’s experience points, but for an ordinary girl to suddenly witness a massacre right in front of her eyes and then personally participate in the slaughter to raise her level, I think the stimulation would be a little too strong. Everything needs to be done in steps. First, she needs to get used to killing centipedes.

I lie in wait for the adventurers coming at us from behind, and as soon as we meet, I use my intimidation skill on them.

「Hey, try to follow us any further. I’ll kill you.」

「Ah.」

「Hii.」

The three men become pale-faced. If they don’t heed my warning and continue to tail us, at that time, I will not show any mercy.

We keep walking for a while, but in the end, they never show themselves. Still, the intimidation skill sure is handy. Let’s use it from now on, too.

「Oops, looks like we’re running into them already.」

I spot two centipedes. They’re clinging to the wall. I put the map into my storage and take out my sword.

The centipedes’ ranks are 2 and 3. Let’s observe them for a bit. When they notice us, they move to the ground and charge towards us. They’re only about as fast as someone walking at a brisk pace, so you can easily run away from them. The standard strategy would be to cut off their countless legs and attack their main body at the end, but as a test, I’ll try moving quickly and cutting off their heads.

「Geh.」

As expected, they have incredible vitality. Even when I appraise them, it says they’re not dead. However, having their heads cut off, they don’t seem to be able to tell where we are, so I guess the fight is pretty much over.

「Michelle, stab the centipede with this.」

「Y, yes.」

I take Michelle’s shield and hand her an iron spear.

Michelle, who has no strength, seems to be barely capable of holding the spear. She launches a thrust at them, but has trouble hitting them.

「Huff, huff.」

「Calm down, these guys have lost their heads and are already near death. Just keep your distance and stab them once at a time.」

She somehow manages to stab them. And then I finish the centipedes off. It seems that they’re still alive even after I cut them in half. Talk about tenacious.

I see, centipedes seem to be monsters that specialize in vitality. As long as you keep your distance, you won’t get hit by their attacks, so for rookie adventurers, I think they’re very sweet opponents. Maybe this labyrinth isn’t so bad. The risk of dying is extremely low, or so I thought, but then a bee flies over with a buzzing sound.

I quickly swing my sword and cut it in half. After appraising it, I find that it’s a toothed bee.

Hmm, these guys might be surprisingly troublesome. Even though bees make a buzzing sound, they fly at you from above. The labyrinth is bright on the ground and the area around it, but it’s dim above, and bees move erratically, making it hard to hit them. Furthermore, in this labyrinth, there are red dogs that move quickly on the ground. If a bee and a red dog appear at the same time and attack from above and below, it will probably be difficult for a rookie adventurer to deal with them. And when you’re preoccupied with the bees or the dogs, you might have a centipede coming at you next. I have to protect Michelle, so I can’t let my guard down either.

「Alright, Michelle, I’ll give you a knife. Try dismantling it.」

「Yes.」

I thought she would dislike it, but Michelle does her best to follow my instructions and take out the magic stone from the monsters. Since she cooks every day, she isn’t so bad with her hands. All that’s left is to dismantle the fur and meat of the red dog, and then to see if she can take out the magic stone from the humanoid goblin. From the way she acted just now, Michelle has the drive at least, and will probably be able to handle it somehow. For the sake of Cordis, she is probably desperate, what a caring elder sister.

「Alright, let’s end it here for today.」

A few hours after going into the labyrinth. After going through many battles, Michelle’s level has gone up to 5. After lunch, it’s still past noon, but I decide to head back for today. That’s because Michelle, who is exploring the labyrinth for the first time wearing equipment she doesn’t normally wear, looks pretty tired. There’s no need to rush.

Besides, I could sense Michelle’s enthusiasm. She’s probably desperate and is doing her best to learn the trade.

We return to the above ground and sell the materials at the Adventurer’s Association. On our way home, I pull out some weeds that catch my eye by the roots. When we get home, it’s time to practice making medicine.

「Alright, Michelle. Normally you have to work under the instructions of a leech, but I’ll teach you the basics of medicine making.」

I’m not knowledgeable about the detailed medicine compounding, but you don’t need to be a leech to be able to make medicine ingredients from raw materials. You use water magic to extract the moisture and medicinal properties from the roots. Then use fire and wind magic to create warm air infused with magical energy to dry them.

「Michelle, you can use fire and water magic, right? Can you use earth and wind magic?」

「Um, I don’t think I can. Since I’ve never used it before.」

「I see.」

Michelle uses magic for daily stuff, such as to make fire and do the dishes, so she probably hasn’t used earth or wind magic, which are not necessary for daily life. She’s a magician, so she’ll probably be able to use it soon, I think.

「You can just learn it little by little. First of all, extraction using water magic. Watch closely.」

I channel my magical energy into the roots of the weed and extract the water inside. It’s pretty hard. I don’t think you’ll be able to do it with ordinary methods. As expected, Michelle seems to be struggling.

「I think the first step is to channel your magical energy into the root and feel the water in the weed. Practice for a while. Alright, Cody, let’s train.」

「Yay.」

Michelle is practicing making medicine inside the house, so Cody and I have a sword fight a little distance away from the house. As usual, his sword strikes are good, but his movements aren’t very good.

「What’s wrong, Cody?」

「Umm, my muscles are a little sore.」

「Ah, you were making movements you were not accustomed to, so it made your muscles sore. At a time like this, it’s better to rest. That’s right, let’s practice stepping in.」

I have Cody, who is having sore muscles, practice stepping in. Even in boxing, what’s important is the movement of your lower body, so it should be good for his future.

After working up a sweat for a while, we return to the house. Michelle seems to be struggling with a weed in her hands. Well, I doubt she will come to be able to do it right away.

「Michelle, you can continue after dinner. I’ll leave dinner to you.」

「Huh, ah, yes. I totally forgot about it. I’ll get it ready right away.」

She must have been very focused. It seems that she has been so focused in her practice that she lost track of time. Skills partly depend on the person’s aptitude, but I get the feeling that a large part of it is also influenced by motivation. At this rate, I think it won’t take too long for her to be able to do it.

After finishing our dinner, we put Cody to bed, and then start treating Michelle’s peach poison again today. I didn’t know that treating illnesses was this difficult. I’m a porter, so I don’t have much magical energy to begin with, but not only do I have high proficiency levels in magical energy manipulation and healing magic, I have a high level, so I believe I’m pretty good at healing magic. And yet, today, too, I failed to complete the treatment. The pink bruise is gone, but when I appraise her, I find that she’s still contracting the disease.

「Amazing, it’s cured.」

「Nah, even though it looks cured on the surface, it’s not completely cured yet. Let’s see, if all goes well, maybe it will be cured by tomorrow.」

「Sei-san, truly, I don’t know how to thank you…」

Michelle becomes teary-eyed and looks at me with her cheeks blushing a little. Well, you could say that I’m her savior, after all.

「Michelle, as I said yesterday, I’m doing this because it’s beneficial for me too. My experience in treating illnesses will surely be very useful to me, after all. You can just thank me when you’re cured. Then we won’t owe each other anything.」

「Sei-san…」

Hmm, these are the eyes of a maiden in love. Michelle is cute and has a good personality. However, she has a little brother she has to look after, and above all else, she is totally unfit for combat, so I just can’t take her on my journey. If I were to judge that Niinya is not suited to be an adventurer, I wouldn’t be able to go on a journey with her either. Well, Niinya is tough enough to go into the labyrinth without a job, so there’s no need to worry about that, though.

「Don’t fall for me, Michelle. I’ll go on a journey sooner or later. And that’ll be the end of it.」

「No way, Sei-san, together…」

「No can do. After diving into the labyrinth today, you get it, don’t you? To put it bluntly, you’re a burden.」

「… Yes.」

「I’m going to sleep now. Good night, Michelle.」

「Good night, Sei-san.」

I cancel my light magic, lie down, and close my eyes, but I can feel Michelle’s gaze. She’s probably worried about me, but I have no intention of reciprocating her feelings.

After a while, Michelle begins to breathe peacefully in her sleep. Having gone into the labyrinth for the first time, she must be pretty exhausted, both mentally and physically. Alright, I guess I should go to sleep too.

In preparation for tomorrow, I fall into a deep sleep.

+++

## 147 - **Complete Recovery**

The morning sun shines into my eyes through the gaps in the house and I wake up. Michelle’s breathing is peacefully in her sleep next to me. Michelle must have been very tired yesterday, so although it would usually be time for her to prepare breakfast, I’ll let her sleep a little longer.

Just a bit; With that in mind, I run my hand along Michelle’s chest as she sleeps, rubbing her breasts and playing with her nipples in a dreamy state. They’re in nice condition. Just as I’m thinking of going back to sleep as is, there’s a loud sound of the door getting banged.

「Hey, you bastard, open up!」

It’s that guy again, huh. The gall he has to disturb my sleep. Still, he’s so energetic so early in the morning. No, maybe he’s been managing the prostitutes all night and is stopping here on his way home after work. I wonder if he lives a life where days and nights are reversed.

「Hmm…」

Michelle starts to wake up. Sigh, Michelle must be tired, so I was thinking about letting her sleep a little longer, and yet, that bastard… I vigorously get up and open the front door.

「Hey, you bastard, the gall you have to make so much noise early in the morning. I’m gonna send you flying for real.」

「Hehehe, kid. That’s the last time you can act so high and mighty. I’m counting on you, big bro.」

「Yeah, so it’s you. The one who poached the prostitute from our house.」

「Huh?」

The collector guy brought along a guy he referred to as big bro. Even though he got so scared of me yesterday, now, borrowing the power of a tiger, he’s putting on a triumphant face. So annoying.

When I appraise this big bro, I find that he’s a level 18 pugilist. I can’t let my guard down, but I don’t think I’ll lose against him.

「Sigh, what do you mean by poached? Michelle can’t do business anymore because of the peach poison, so she’s decided to earn money for her treatment by doing odd jobs for me. Just leave her alone already.」

「As if that will do. She can still earn money, so we won’t give her to you. Now, we’ll be taking her back.」

「Michelle doesn’t belong to you, does he? Just who do you think you are?」

「Kid, looks like you don’t get it. We’re from the Bartalis family, you know?」

The Bartalis family, huh. I believe they’re the guys who control the slums. If possible, I don’t want to make an enemy of them, but in proportion to the level of the labyrinth here, there don’t seem to be many skilled guys in this town, so I don’t think they’re much of a threat. Besides, we haven’t done anything wrong. Dealing with idiots is really exhausting.

「I don’t know who you guys are, but Michelle won’t do business anymore. Just give up.」

「So he says, big bro.」

「Sigh, I guess there’s no other way.」

The pugilist and I glare at each other. If I draw my sword, I’ll probably end up going all the way, so I guess I’ll use body enhancement and fight with my bare hands. If you were to fight a pugilist with your bare hands, normally, you wouldn’t stand a chance. However, given how high my level is, if I use full strength body enhancement on my strength, I think I’ll manage one way or another. This guy is probably fairly skilled, but I don’t feel any awe-inspiring air that is characteristic of a powerhouse.

「…Tch, hey, let’s go.」

「Huh, big bro?! Damn it, kid, just you wait!」

After glaring at each other for a while, this big bro guy walks away. What a sharp guy. He seems to have realized that I’m someone he won’t be able to deal with by ordinary means. I’m over 180 cm tall, about 10 cm taller than him, after all. There are no classes in a fistfight. Basically, the bigger one has the advantage. Still, thank goodness it didn’t turn into a battle to the death with the gangsters. I’ve had enough of troublesome stuff, after all.

As we eat breakfast, we discuss our plans from now on.

「Michelle, Cody, we may have to leave this town soon. Listen, if you still have some business here, take care of it. However, don’t let anyone know you’re leaving. There might be people like those guys who will try to keep you here, after all.」

「Yes.」

「Got it.」

Neither Michelle nor Cody seem to have any particular attachment to this town. I wonder if they have no relatives either. Let’s try asking Michelle about it during our break in the labyrinth later.

After finishing our breakfast, we buy some food and head to the labyrinth. There are a lot of adventurers hanging around in front of the labyrinth entrance, probably for meetings or rendezvous, and as usual, Michelle and I end up getting stared at scrutinizingly by them. In this garbage dump, they probably see me as a rich young master, and Michelle as a target to be raped.

Well then, after a day of exploring the labyrinth yesterday, I was able to complete a large part of the map for the area around the entrance. Today let’s try going much further in. If we are ever attacked, I will show no mercy. I thought about turning the attackers into Michelle’s experience points, but she is going to be a leech’s assistant. She is not an adventurer, so I don’t think she needs experience in killing. I will take care of all of them. We set foot into the labyrinth.

Sigh, good grief. As expected, it looks like we are being followed. Three, or perhaps four people? More than five is unlikely, I’d say. I don’t think there are too many of them. In this labyrinth, you don’t need that many people, and the more people you have, the smaller your share will be. There is no point in working with an unnecessarily large number of people.

What should I do? If a monster were to attack us from behind while I’m dealing with those guys, Michelle might end up getting hurt. If we were unlucky, the worst could even happen. At any rate, since Michelle is with me, I don’t think it’s impossible for us to get away from them. In that case, let’s try to lure them to a place that would be advantageous to us. It’s a good thing I’ve made a map. I check the map and head to the dead end.

「Michelle, in a bit, I’m going to fight some robbers. You stay here.」

「Huh?」

「Listen, if you move carelessly, it’ll put me in trouble. So make sure not to move at all.」

「Y, yes. I understand.」

Michelle doesn’t seem to realize we are being followed. Yes, monsters aren’t the only danger in the labyrinth. It would serve as a good experience for Michelle… No, it’s not like she’s going to become an adventurer. She probably doesn’t need this kind of experience in her life, so I guess it would be best to fight them somewhere as far away from her as possible.

I go back the way we came by myself and confront the trio of adventurers. Appraisal! Alright, they’re not that big of a deal.

「Hey, you guys, this is a dead end. Turn back.」

「Is that so? From now on, this road is closed. If you want to pass, you’ll have to pay a toll.」

「That’s right, give us all of your equipment, luggage, and clothes. We’ll let you keep your underwear at least.」

「Hey, where’s the woman? Tch, looks like she’s hiding.」

Now then, let’s do it. It’s probably because I’m young and it’s three against one, these guys have a relaxed look on their faces and are letting their guard down. If all three of them were to slash at me at once, they might have a chance, and yet…

「Huh?」

I use instant step, followed by a high-speed horizontal slash to send the head of the man on the far right flying. Unable to react, he makes a stupid noise, and breathes his last.

「Ah…」

Then the second one. I slash at the guy in the middle. He reacts slightly, but I strongly push his sword back. It seems he wasn’t prepared for combat. He doesn’t put much strength into his hand that’s holding the sword, so I succeed in knocking it off. He’s now left unarmed, so I send his head flying without panicking. With this, we’re good.

I won’t kill the third person yet. I’m going to gather information, after all.

「Wha—, no way, why, why…」

「Shut up. You’ll scare the woman. The next time you say anything uncalled for, I’ll send your head flying. Got it?」

I hold my sword to his throat and threaten him. The man bobs his head up and down frantically. Next to him is the body of his comrade, bleeding profusely from the now headless neck, and it could be him in a few seconds. His face turns pale, and he lets go of the sword. He has completely lost his will to fight.

「If you answer my questions honestly, I’ll let you live. If you lie, I’ll kill you right away. Got it?」

I threaten him, pressing my sword against his throat and cutting his skin a little. The man bobs his head up and down frantically. Naturally, I have no intention of letting him live.

「Why did you follow us?」

「Ah, about that, umm, a rookie adventurer was taking along a beautiful woman with him, so…」

I knew it. But there’s nothing we can do about this one thing. The most we can do is hide her face, I’d say. Or maybe we should go to the labyrinth earlier, nah, I can’t get up any earlier than this. Rather than that, maybe it’s better to go a little later. Now then, the other information that I need…

「Do you know about the Bartalis family?」

「Y, yeah, of course. They’re the guys who control the slums, no?」

「How many members do they have?」

「As if I’d know. There are a lot of them.」

「Are there any hostile forces?」

「No, never heard of them.」

「I see, thanks for your cooperation.」

「Gaba.」

I cut off his head. I didn’t get any particularly useful information. It was a complete waste of time. Now then, let’s continue to raise Michelle’s level.

「Michelle, keep your eyes half-closed and walk this way without looking down.」

In the area around the entrance and stairs of the labyrinth, there’s a good chance that we’ll run into other adventurers, so I guess we need to get away from here as soon as possible.

I start walking towards the deeper parts of the first stratum with Michelle.

◇ ◇ ◇

「Alright, it looks like you’ve gotten used to dismantling. Let’s take a short break.」

「Yes.」

With beads of sweat on her forehead, Michelle finished dismantling the red dog that I had defeated. After dismantling it, she uses water magic to create water and wipes off the dirt. She’s dexterous. Not only does she do her job single-mindedly and without complaint, she’s beautiful, has a good personality, and is quite good-looking. As expected, the slums just don’t suit her.

I sit down, take out some fruit from my storage, and ask her about her circumstances while munching on it.

「Are your parents no longer around, Michelle?」

「Yes, my mother passed away two years ago. As for my father, I’ve never seen him, not even once. Most likely, we’re children that my mother had as she did her business.」

I see, so her mother was also a prostitute. Judging from the atmosphere of the house, it seems that she earned a fairly good amount of money.

In this world, there are birth control pills. Prostitutes with a fair amount of money to spare would normally take birth control pills, so if she gave birth to Michelle and Cordis, she probably got pregnant on purpose. One way or another, she found out that her client was of noble birth, and secretly did so so that her child would be granted a high-ranked job. If that’s the case, it makes sense that she, a commoner, was granted the job of magician, which is common among the nobility. Maybe Cordis will also be granted a good job when he comes of age.

We hunt monsters until before dusk, then head to the Adventurer’s Association.

The three walk deeper into the back alley. I follow them while concealing my presence.

This area is away from the main street, so there are no people around. Let’s do it, shall we? It doesn’t matter even if someone sees it. They probably won’t be able to see my face in this darkness, and even if they do find out, we’ll leave this town tomorrow.

Now then, let’s leave the collector alone and deal with the two who are likely combat personnel. I don’t mind beating them up half-dead, but let’s render them incapable of fighting first.

I take out my mithril alloy iron ball from my storage and channel my magical energy into it. It looks like they don’t notice. It seems they don’t have magical energy perception skill. My first targets are those two. One is the pugilist man I met the other day. The other is a man with a sword hanging from his waist. In such a narrow alley, fists might be more of a threat than a sword. It would be troublesome if he got close. I aim at the pugilist man and throw the iron ball from behind him.

「Guo…Gabaa!」

「Huh, big bro?!」

「What, what’s wrong?」

What a slow bunch. In the dark alley, they have no idea what happened to their friend who suddenly collapsed. Well, as they don’t have any enemy organizations and they can do whatever they want, they probably wouldn’t expect to be attacked from behind at night.

Instant step. I close in on the man with the sword at high speed.

「You bastard, who the hell are…Guha!」

He notices me approaching from behind, but the moment he draws his sword, I cut his arm. I follow up with a thrust into his stomach with my mithril sword, impaling him. It’s a fatal wound. If he has neither healing magic nor potions, he will probably die before long. Well, enjoy the agony until you die.

「Hiiii, you bastard, what are you doing, we’re Bar… Hiii.」

「If you say anything unnecessary, I’ll kill you. Answer my question.」

I put my sword to the collector’s neck and threaten him. He’s a coward, so most likely, he will no longer put up any resistance. His two dying comrades are groaning beside him.

「Ah, I, I get it. I’ll tell you anything. Please, don’t kill me.」

「Why did you kill Cordis?」

「Cordis?」

「Michelle’s little brother.」

「Ah, that guy. Huh? You bastard, you’re that guy from back then, aren’t you? Do you know who I am… Guha!」

I cut off the collector’s right wrist. It’s really tiring to deal with idiots. They forget their place so quickly.

「It hurts, my hand, my hand…」

「The next time you say something unnecessary, I’ll chop off your left wrist. Got it?」

「Ah, ah.」

The collector nods his head frantically. He’s finally obedient. Now then.

「So, why did you kill Cordis?」

「Y, you’ve got it wrong. We didn’t mean to kill him. When the three of us visited Michelle’s house, he was there, and he told us not to lay a hand on his elder sister, and then…」

「And then?」

「He charged at us with a wooden sword, and then big bro and the other guy fought him, but he was stronger than we thought… Say, please, at this rate, I’m going to die. Let me stop the bleeding, I beg you.」

It seems like he knows he’s on the brink of death. He probably thinks he’ll be killed if he tells me everything. If he did, perhaps the one who could talk would no longer be able to.

Let’s use healing magic on the collector’s right wrist and stop the bleeding. For now, I should focus on extracting information.

「See, the bleeding has stopped. You didn’t lay a hand on Cordis, did you? In that case if you tell me everything, I’ll spare your life. So, what happened?」

「Y, you’re not lying, right? Ah, then that kid attacked big bro with a wooden sword, and big and the other guy fought back, but that kid started using instant step and body strengthening, and perhaps swordsmanship skill too, so they couldn’t hold back.」

I see, as I thought, it seems Cordis had a talent for combat. His skills might have blossomed as he fought desperately in order to protect Michelle.

「No matter how many times big bro hit him, he kept coming at us, so… they went at it until the very end. Hey, please be understanding. We really didn’t mean to kill him. We work to pay money to the higher-ups, you see. Killing some kid won’t earn us a single penny. Killing him left nothing but a bad aftertaste in our mouth, so….」

There doesn’t seem to be any contradiction in what he’s saying. What should I do? Should I kill these three and satisfy myself? Or…

「Hey, where is your leader right now?」

「Huh, Boss is at the headquarters office most of the time, but… Oi, don’t tell me, you’d better not get any weird ideas. Perish the thought, alright?」

The Bartalis family will probably be raided by the Knights and slaughtered anyway, but if I can, I want to get rid of them. Let’s raid their headquarters now. If it looks like it will work, I’ll kill all of them, including the boss. If it looks difficult, I’ll just make my escape at the right moment. For the time being, I have to take a look at the actual site. Besides, I don’t have enough information.

「How many guards are there at the headquarters?」

「Hey, like I told you, you should perish… Hiii.」

I press my sword against his neck and make him bleed a little. I can kill him now, but let’s make him spill all the information he has.

「If you don’t answer my question, I’ll kill you. So, how many guards are there?」

「U, usually, there are two or three guards on the external stairs on the ground floor. And then, two guards in front of the iron door in front of the headquarters on the third floor.」

「External stairs? I heard there’s a tavern on the first floor, though?」

「Yeah, you can also get there from the internal stairs in the tavern, but when you go to the office, you usually go from the external stairs.」

「Why are there only that many guards?」

「Well, there’s no one in this town who would attack the boss, so the number of guards is kept to the minimum, and most of the gang members stay in the tavern or guardroom, and are only called out and mobilized when they’re needed.」

「Then, are there any skilled guys?」

「Err, there are a few guys who are around the same level as big bro.」

Around the same level as these guys who are lying on the ground next to me right now, groaning and unable to die, huh. I think I’ll manage somehow.

「But the boss has one very skilled bodyguard.」

「Hoh~, what kind of guy is he?」

「I don’t know much about him, but I heard he’s a former silver rank adventurer and a master swordsman.」

That guy sounds troublesome. However, there’s only one strong opponent, huh. If I can catch him off guard, I should be able to kill him. Besides, my proficiency level in swordsmanship is 6. Combined with my body strengthening, I should be able to fight him on equal terms. He probably won’t leave the boss’s side, so if things get dangerous, I think I will be able to run away.

After thinking about it for a while, I decided to let the collector live for a while. He might still be useful. I cut off the heads of the two men, who are on the verge of death and crawling on the ground. Just to be safe. After all, if they survive and go around spreading words that I’m a murderer, it’ll be troublesome. I can’t afford to let them live.

「Hii~, y, you killed them. That’s…」

「Shut up, a yakuza shouldn’t be scared of something like murder. Now, take me to the headquarters. No need to worry, I have no intention of killing you, after all. Ah, if you try to run away, I’ll definitely kill you. I’ll cut off your limbs and kill you. I’ll find you and kill you no matter what. Now, get going.」

「Y, yes.」

With the collector guy in the lead, I head to the headquarters of the Bartalis family. Now then, God only knows what may happen. Depending on how things go, I’ll beat a retreat straight away. If it looks like I will work, I’ll kill them all with these two hands of mine.

+++

## 151 - **Retribution 2**

「Hey, what’s the meaning of this?」

「Hiii.」

I point my sword at the collector’s neck.

Having this guy lead the way, I’ve come close to the headquarters of the Bartalis family, but it’s different from what he said. There are about ten men hanging out at the entrance to the external stairs. Damn it, it’s not only two or three.

「I don’t know, I swear. Maybe some of the executives have come.」

「If the executives have come, the boss is surely there, right?」

「Y, yeah. Well, I suppose so, but please spare me, seriously. I’ll get into trouble too.」

No need to worry about getting into trouble, as I’ll definitely kill you, after all. Be useful until you die.

「Alright, go gather information from those guys about how many executives have come. I’ll pretend to be your underling and follow you from behind. If you do anything strange, I’ll stab you from behind.」

「Hii, I get it, I get it, alright?」

Hiding myself with my cloak, I point my sword at the collector’s back.

Due to the fact that it’s late at night, there are no street lights, and we’re in front of a yakuza headquarters, there are no people around at all. One of the guards is illuminating the area with light magic, but that’s the only source of light.

The inside of the first floor of the building seems to be a tavern, so I can hear the voices of people talking, but the entrance is located in a different place, and they’re making merry inside, so we probably won’t be found if we get into a fight at the outside staircase. It’s easy to erase your presence in this darkness, so it’s easy to run away.

Hiding behind the collector, I approach them.

「Hey, brother.」

「Huh? Who are you?」

「Ah, I’m the person in charge of managing the prostitutes around the main street, but more importantly, what’s with this big crowd? Are the executives gathering or something?」

「Yeah, today is the executive meeting day. All six of them have come. You too, if you don’t have any business here…」

Executive meeting? All the executives are here, huh. That could be said to be a good opportunity, but as expected, it might be difficult to fight all of the executives at once. I wonder if those guys are strong.

Now then, there are eleven of them in total. No one notices even when I appraise them, and there are no high-leveled ones. Above all else, they are completely not on guard against their surrounding area and not ready for battle.

I look around. As expected, there is no one around and it’s quiet. Well, I guess there’s no one who would willingly wander around a yakuza headquarters late at night. Alright, let’s do it.

「Gah… Ouch!」

I kick the collector towards the men from behind. The men focus their attention on the collector who fell to the ground while letting out a loud cry. In that instant, I use full-strength body enhancement, channel my magical energy into my mithril sword, and send the heads of those guys flying.

「Gah.」

「What?!」

「Gugah.」

「Gah…」

Not only am I able to catch them off guard, the men are not ready for battle at all. When I cut off the head of the one who is using light magic, the area is shrouded in darkness, and the men fall into panic and are unable to grasp the situation. I cut them down mercilessly.

Seven, eight, nine. Two more. As expected, the last two are ready for battle. I can’t back down at this point. I’ll finish them off in one go.

The technique I learned from Nakulus, the pugilist from the Cotton Clouds, comes in handy. Using body manipulation, I channel magical energy into my brain and increase my processing power. This puts a lot of strain on the brain, so I need to finish the battle in a short time.

The man on the right puts his hand on the hilt of his sword. The man on the left assumes a boxing stance. He must be a pugilist. It doesn’t go as far as slow motion, but time feels slow, slow enough to allow me to think about my next move. There’s no need to kill them in one hit. Rendering them incapable of fighting is my top priority.

I use my mithril sword to swipe the fingers of the man on the right who is trying to draw his sword. Four fingers fall off cleanly. With this, his fighting power is now less than half. And then, the man on the left, if he’s a pugilist, I should be careful of his foot movement rather than his fists. I immediately swing my sword at the pugilist’s thigh. I need to conserve my stamina and magical energy, so I cancel the body manipulation on my brain.

「Guaah.」

「D, damn it.」

I decapitate the man who can’t draw his sword and the pugilist who is on his knees. And then, I finish off all the guys who are still alive. Phew, no one has noticed. So far so good.

「Hiiiiii, ahh, you’ve gone and done it now….」

「Hey, don’t make a fuss. Someone might come.」

「Y, yes.」

I make the collector calm down. This area is shrouded in darkness, but the bodies of the eleven men are splattered all over the place. The collector is unable to stand up due to fear. Given things, he probably won’t run away.

What should I do? If the executive meeting is being held, there’s a chance someone will come here. I put the chopped up bodies of the eleven men into my storage. Even if the ground is wet with blood, they probably won’t notice in this darkness.

「Huh?! You were a porter?」

Shoot. The fact that I’m a porter has ended up being exposed to the collector. Well, I guess it’s about time. Let’s extract some information for the last time.

「The headquarters is on the third floor, right? What about the second floor up the stairs?」

「The second floor is the guard area. There should be a lot of gang members waiting there, including the executives’ underlings.」

This is bad, as expected, it’s too dangerous to deal with such a large group of people. I guess this is as far as I can go.

「Do you have to go through the guard area to get to the third floor?」

「No, you can go through the hallway and reach the stairs to the third floor. The guard area is inside the room.」

I see. If all goes well, I can get to the third floor without running into anyone. They must’ve never thought that someone would break into a yakuza headquarters. He said there were no rival organizations, after all.

In that case, if I’m lucky, I’ll only have to deal with the guards guarding the iron door on the third floor. If that’s the case, even if it’s just to check what the situation is like, let’s go in for now.

「Hey, please. That’s enough already, no? I’ll pretend I didn’t see anything, so please let me go.」

「Yeah, I suppose so, thanks for everything.」

「Gaah.」

I behead the collector and then put his body into my storage. By all rights, I would have made him suffer the pain of hell before killing him, but not only did he seem to not have any intention of killing Cordis, he’d been useful in many ways, so I killed him in one fell swoop.

「Phew.」

I steady my breath. I have plenty of magical energy left. My automatic recovery is also working. I can do it.

I recall the meeting of Japanese yakuza executives. When the boss and the executives gather, they don’t bring guns or knives. It’s because they trust each other. In other words, right now, where the executive meeting is underway, in which there’s a good chance they’re unarmed, is the perfect opportunity.

I step towards the stairs.

+++

## 152 - **Retribution 3**

I climb the stairs, step by step. Strangely, I don’t feel any nervousness. Maybe it’s because I know that when push comes to shove, I’ll be able to escape in the darkness of the night, and because my spirits have shot through the roof after killing eleven people.

I take a breath and steel myself. Just to be safe, I use presence concealment halfway up the stairs, and make it to the top of the stairs.

「It’s just as the information I got.」

It’s just as the collector said. The second floor, lit by the magical lighting, has several doors, and the inside seems to be the guard area of the gang members. Fortunately, there are no people on the stairs or in the hallway, where I’m currently at. After walking a little down the hallway, I find the stairs to the third floor. From here, I have to be careful. If the information is correct, the third floor is the office headquarters, and the leader as well as the six executives of the Bartalis family should be there now. And then, there are two guards guarding the iron door to the room.

As expected, I’m starting to get nervous. I can feel my heart beating faster and my mouth getting dry.

I go up the stairs. While erasing my presence, I pass the landing, crouch and climb carefully.

I check the situation on the third floor. Alright, there’s no entrance directly in front of the stairs. It looks like I won’t suddenly run into the guards. I go to the top of the stairs and pop my head out for a moment to peer down the hallway. It’s just as the information I got. On either side of the iron door, there are two men with swords hanging from their waists. Not good, I only peeked for a moment, but I wonder if they noticed me. For some reason, I get the feeling that one of the guards has shifted his gaze this way. Is it just my imagination?

I use body manipulation to control my senses, especially my hearing. Some time passes, but there’s no sign that they’re going to make some kind of action.

In the first place, the idea of their lives being targeted probably never crosses their minds. It’s unclear whether the guards are skilled or not, but they’re standing in front of the iron door simply because it’s their job, and I don’t think they’re ready to engage in a battle to the death for real as an assassin comes at them.

If that’s the case, then maybe I should just boldly walk up to them, draw my sword, and cut them down in a surprise attack.

No, they’re stationed on either side of the iron door. In that case, my specialty, the iron ball attack, should be a good choice here. The two of them are in a straight line, so it’s easy to aim. It allows me to attack from medium range, so I can easily escape even if I fail. But I would end up leaving the mithril alloy iron ball behind. No, I also have the reward for discovering the eleventh stratum of the Puppet Labyrinth. I have plenty of money. I ought to choose the ease of escape over the possibility of losing a single iron ball.

Just to be safe, I swallow one magical energy restorative medicine. I take out the iron ball from my storage and begin to fill it with magical energy. There’s no sign of them moving. I’m done charging it with magical energy. What should I do, should I jump out all at once? No, it might make them wary of me. Let’s pretend to be a gang member and walk over slowly. My heart is beating fast with tension. Calm down, it’s something I do all the time, isn’t it? I focus on my throwing skill. Alright, let’s go.

I climb the stairs and walk slowly down the third-floor hallway. They turn their gazes at me. It seems they aren’t wary of me at all.

「Hmm? Who are you?」

「Err, the guard told me to bring you some midnight snacks.」

「Oh, that’s very thoughtful of you…」

Holding the iron ball in a way so that these guys won’t be able to see it, I use a big motion to give it momentum and throw it at one of them.

「Ugh?!」

Perhaps by reflex, the guard dodges the ball by a hair’s breadth. But…

「Gaba!」

My aim is the face of the man on the back, who has been in the line of fire from the start. It hits the mark splendidly, and I can hear the dull sound of his skull breaking.

*Clink* A metallic sound rings out. My sword and the guard’s sword meet. Worthily the guard of the executive, he seems to be different from a small fry. The sword is made of red iron, and magical energy passes through it a moment later. His ability to manipulate magical energy doesn’t seem to be that great.

「You bastard, hey! Someone… Ugh!」

I switch into a series of attacks with my sword. He’s about to call out for help, so I don’t give him the time to do so. My swordsmanship skill is superior to his, and he can do nothing but defend himself.

「Ah, kuh, hey, wait…」

It’s completely one sided, so it’s only a matter of time before the battle comes to an end. Continuing to use body enhancement like this will consume a lot of magical energy. I immediately throw a kick at him.

I then move to his side with instant step, and unleash a horizontal slash at his neck.

「Ugh?!」

I wonder if it’s what people called: a cornered rat will bite a cat. My sword cuts off his neck, but he unleashes a swing with all his might and hits my neck. Not good, I put my hand to the wound. A potion…

It seems the wound is shallow, and not deep enough to cut a large blood vessel. Result-wise, I was able to beat the two guards, but perhaps I rushed the battle too much. If I had been unlucky, I might have suffered a fatal injury.

There is no time to relax. I put the two bodies and the iron ball into my storage, and just to be safe, I drink a stamina restorative medicine.

I kill the noise and concentrate my nerves. There is no change on the third or second floor. Getting into a battle, we ended up making some noise, but we were separated from the room on the third floor by this iron door. Perhaps it has some soundproofing effect.

Still, what should I do about this iron door? As expected, it would be difficult to destroy. If I use my mithril alloy sledgehammer, I will probably be able to destroy it. However, doing that would naturally raise suspicion, and everyone inside would get ready for battle

What should I do, should I just go back? But I have come this far. I want to put an end to the life of Bartalis, the boss of those who killed Cordis and are treating Michelle and the prostitutes roughly, with these two hands of mine. I hesitate for a moment, and then I hear a clang and the iron door slowly begins to open.

Not good! What should I do? If I want to run away, now is my only chance. However…

+++

## 153 - **Retribution 4**

The inner lock is opened with a click, the knob of the iron door turns with a clank, and it starts to open.

What to do? This is a good chance to slaughter them all, but it’s also very risky. If I’m not going to do it, I should beat a retreat right this instant, but… Damn it, what should I do? I can’t make up my mind.

「Hey, you’re being too noisy, what in the world is… Hmm? Who are you?」

A fierce-looking man comes out from inside. Judging from his attitude and the fine clothes he’s wearing, he must be one of the executives. I hesitate and end up getting my face seen. There’s no other choice but to do it, prepare yourself, me.

「Huh… Gah?!」

I swing my sword at the man’s defenseless neck. The man holds the wound, but he’s bleeding profusely, so I don’t think he will last long. Normally, I should leave the door open so I can escape at any time, but the people downstairs might notice the abnormal event and send reinforcements.

I grab the man whose neck I have cut and push my way into the room.

I look around the room. A slightly overweight man sitting opposite the entrance in the center of the spacious room, that guy must be Bartalis. And then, there are three chairs on either side of the table, with three people sitting on the right and two on the left. The one sitting in the empty seat on the left is probably this man whose neck I have cut. And then, a man with long blonde hair sitting against the wall a distance away from Bartalis and the others, that guy is probably the bodyguard who is a former silver rank adventurer.

It seems that they don’t grasp what’s going on yet. The man whose neck has been cut off is unable to speak, after all.

My eyes meet those of Bartalis. The other five aren’t wary of me. There’s no turning back now, I’ll do it, I’m definitely going to kill him.

I throw the man I’m holding to the side and use instant step to charge at Bartalis in one go.

「You bastard, who are you…」

Bartalis stands up and quickly escapes backwards. Jumping onto the table using the momentum of the instant step, I then make another jump… or so I’d like to. The bodyguard man closes in on me with instant step and tries to block my way. That movement, he is no ordinary person. He pulls out his rapier and thrusts it at me.

Damn it, I can’t kill Bartalis. In that case…

I forcefully deflect the bodyguard’s sword, quickly move backwards, and decapitate the five executives who still don’t grasp what’s going on. I finish off the executives who are about to drink potions, then face the bodyguard man.

「You bastard! Who the hell are you?! The gall you have to do something like this, don’t think you’ll be able to get away with it!」

Bartalis yells from behind the bodyguard man, but for now I need to focus on the man in front of me. If I can kill him, all that’s left will be that guy. I can do it.

I use Appraisal, but it ends up getting repelled by the bodyguard man. He’s got a rather impressive magical energy manipulation skill. However, it looks like I’m superior to him in it. As the man tries to deflect my Appraisal, I forcefully activate my Appraisal with my high proficiency magical energy manipulation. Appraisal!

Dinos Zentrigers, Age 37, Level 40

Job: Swordsman

He has a family name. Is he of noble origin? There’s a good chance that he has a high proficiency level in swordsmanship.

「Tch, appraisal? This battle prowess and magical energy manipulation, you must be a knight…」

「Close but not quite there, I’m a magic knight. Still, for you to be level 40, despite your low-ranking job, you seem pretty good yourself, Dinos.」

For now, let’s bluff our way out. If at all possible, I’d like to avoid combat. I have no idea what status this guy has, but if he’s not a blood relative and is an employed bodyguard, I doubt he’ll risk death to protect his employer to the bitter end. If it looks like he’s going to lose, he might run away before he suffers any injuries.

「It’s not a low-ranking job, it’s a basic job.」

「What’s the difference?」

「You bastard…」

Ah, crap. It looks like I’ve taunted him too much. Even though he’s of noble origin, he became an adventurer instead of a knight, and now he’s working as a bodyguard for the yakuza. He may be a man with various complicated circumstances.

Dinos puts more strength into the hand that’s holding his sword. It looks like a fight is unavoidable.

「Hey! Dinos, I’m paying you a lot of money. I’m counting on you, alright?」

「…..」

I hold my sword at the ready and face Dinos. This feeling, it’s the air of a powerhouse that I haven’t felt in a long time. There’s no room at all to probe his strength or take it easy on him. If I don’t go all out, I’ll get myself killed.

Circulating my magical energy throughout my entire body and the blade of my sword, I activate body enhancement and also channel magical energy into my brain. It’s a short decisive battle. Victory goes to the one who makes the first move!

Without any preparatory motions at all, I use instant movement to swiftly close in on Dinos. I deflect the mithril rapier he is holding to the side…no, I can’t deflect it. He pulls his sword back, and mine cuts through the air. Ah, not good.

「Haaah!」

「Kuh!」

Dinos launches a thrust at me with his rapier that has been imbued with magical energy. It’s a super-fast thrust, but for me, who has enhanced my brain’s reaction speed, it’s possible to dodge.

「Ugh?!」

Dinos unleashes a series of thrust attacks at me mercilessly.

Not good, his sword strikes are so fast that, although not completely, I can’t counterattack. Dodging and defecting it with my sword, I defend myself against his consecutive thrust attacks. Ugh, not good, I’m channeling magical energy to my whole body, sword, and even my brain, so the magical energy consumption is too severe. However, his attacks never stop, so I have no room to take any other actions. Not good, he’s strong, I can’t beat him. What to do now…?

「Phew—」

If the attacks had continued for a few more seconds, I might not have been able to block them. Dinos stops his attacks for a moment and retreats backwards. As he takes a breather, large beads of sweat begin to form on his forehead.

It seems that not only me, but he too has pushed himself quite a bit to unleash those attacks.

What to do, can I beat him? From the way it felt just now, I’m superior in strength, and I may also be slightly superior in swordsmanship. However, I’m severely lacking in speed. It’s probably a correction as a swordsman, but his agility is far superior to mine. The reason I can barely keep up with his attacks is because I’m enhancing my brain’s reaction time using body enhancement and magical energy manipulation, in which I have a high proficiency level. And that’s putting too much strain on me.

This is bad, maybe the only option left now is to run away. I’ve come this far, but I can’t risk my life. I’ve even had my face seen. I need to leave the town as soon as the gate opens.

「Tch, looks like your claim of being a magic knight was not all talk.」

What to do? For the time being, let’s buy some time with a bluff and recover my strength.

「Naturally, and it just so happens that I was getting tired of fighting small fry. I’m relieved to find someone who can fight a little. So do your best to entertaining me, Dinos.」

「Phew, the heck are you talking about? Even if you’re a magic knight, there’s no way you’d be at a high level at such a young age. I know you have no room to spare either.」

「Good grief, a man with a low-ranking job only has this level of insight, huh.」

「What did you say?」

「I’ve been taking a lot of purple potions, so you might want to stop taking me as someone as young as my appearance tells. Now, come at me.」

「…..」

How’s that? I’ve been fighting and talking with a poker face the whole time, so he must have found it unsettling. He must be having trouble judging how much of what I say is true.

What to do, it’d be an all or nothing gamble, but should I try to attack? He shouldn’t have that much room to spare either. If I’m lucky, I might be able to take him down. I have strength restorative medicines and mid-grade red potions with me, so as long as I don’t take a fatal injury, I should be able to manage one way or another.

I’ve pushed Bartalis this far, let’s do it.

Channeling my magical energy into it, I unleash my intimidation skill at Dinos. Let’s go…

「Wait, I get it.」

「What did you get?」

# The Neighborhood High School Girl, Miss Isezaki, Is the Great Saintess Returned from Another World~ And I, Suddenly Awakened as Her Exclusive Mana Supply Uncle, Travel Between Earth and Another World with Time-Space Magic~ - 203: The Green Garden

As we headed towards the large tree where a lot of medicinal herbs were supposed to grow, Maristel suddenly stopped in her tracks. Her gaze was fixed on a mound of earth.

“…Isn’t that the remains of the golem Matsunaga destroyed?”

“Yes, that’s right. They appeared in greater numbers than expected, so it was quite a hassle.”

“I see… Well, I have something to take care of over here, so you go on ahead~♪”

We entered the shade of the large tree together. As soon as we stepped inside, a pleasant breeze brushed against our cheeks.

It was so cool and calming, and it felt like the fatigue from earlier was melting away. Maybe this is what they call a power spot.

“I see… The flow of magical energy around here is very pure. Perhaps the large tree and the waterfall influence each other,” 

Isezaki-san said, looking around with admiration. Apparently, from a fantasy perspective, it was a very good place.

“Does that mean medicinal herbs grow more easily in places like this?”

“Yes. Look, Master, over here. Most of the plants growing around are well-known medicinal herbs, magical herbs, and spirit herbs.”

“Wow…”

I lowered my gaze to the ground and carefully scanned the area. The lush greenery under the tree was filled with a riot of colorful flowers, all standing tall and vibrant. Maybe it’s because of Isezaki-san’s explanation, but they all seemed like rare herbs.

“Hm… Isezaki-san, what’s this black one…?”

Among them was a plant with unusual black fruit. The fruit was completely black, with no color variations, and seemed particularly extraordinary compared to the others. I instinctively felt it was something that might be exchanged for an equivalent amount of gold.

“That’s a Dogyunza. It’s… well, it’s just a common weed,” 

Isezaki-san answered, averting her eyes and sounding somewhat hesitant. I felt embarrassed for asking with a pretentious attitude. What’s with the ‘hm…’?

“Oh, I see… Then, which medicinal herbs are needed for making potions?!”

To diffuse the awkward atmosphere, I decided to return to the original topic. Isezaki-san, perhaps feeling the same way, clapped her hands and quickly answered.

“That would be… the white-flowered plant growing over there… It’s called the Healer’s Herb. If you collect those, you should be able to make high-quality potions!”

“Got it, then I’ll start right away!”

“Yes! I’ll help!”

We crouched down and quickly began picking the Healer’s Herbs. Let’s see, it’s better not to take the roots, right…

◇◇◇

“Sure, but be quick about it, okay~?”

“Huft, huft… G-go ahead, Husband…”

Maristel pouted in dissatisfaction. Isezaki, drenched in sweat from the climb, saw me off with a resigned expression. With their gazes on me, I headed to the restroom.

I opened the wooden door, quickly slipped inside, and shut the door behind me.

In the dim, cramped space, I stood alone. I stared at the hole in the middle of the wooden board that was likely intended for use as a toilet. Instead of lowering my pants, however, I murmured,

“—[Dimensional Teleport].”

And teleported out of there.

◇◇◇

The place I teleported to using [Dimensional Teleport] was my personal room in the castle assigned to me by Lady Levia.

Of course, it’s not that I have any particular aversion to using the fortress’ restroom.

Since it was decided that we’d be spending the night at the fortress on short notice, I needed to inform someone. More importantly, I’d left Aihara in limbo, and I needed to send her back to Japan before staying the night here.

After ringing the bell in my room, Holly arrived immediately. I already knew she was an efficient maid, but she’s so competent that it’s almost scary.

“Welcome back, Master Matsunaga. …Although, it seems you’re not truly returning home, are you? Did something happen?”

Without missing a beat, the capable maid immediately grasped the situation as soon as she entered the room. She narrowed her eyes while asking why I had come back.

“Yeah, well, various things happened, and we’re staying at the fortress for the night. I came back to send Aihara to Japan first. Sorry, but could you—”

Before I could finish asking her to fetch Aihara, I heard hurried footsteps. Both Aihara and Colin burst into the room.

“Welcome back, Senpai! …Wait, where’s Seina-chan?”

“I just stopped by briefly, so it’s just me. Anyway, we’re staying overnight at the fortress, but… perfect timing. I’m about to send you back to Japan—”

“Ehh!? No way! If Senpai and the others are staying overnight, I want to stay too!”

“Huh? No, no, I can’t bring you to the fortress.”

“What are you talking about, Senpai? I know that much! I meant staying overnight at the castle! So, um… uh… Wata… Toma…”

Aihara paused for a moment, gazing at the ceiling and muttering to herself. She then turned to Holly and said, for some reason in broken language,

“Holly-san, me, castle, stay, can I?”

Holly’s eyes widened as she responded.

“Y-Yes, of course, it’s no problem.”

“Can? Yes! Yay! Thank you, Holly-san!”

Aihara started bouncing with joy, and that’s when I finally realized what was off.

“Wait a sec… you can speak the language here?”

“Yep! I’m still just learning, but Colin-chan’s been showing me around the town and teaching me the language. …Right, Colin-chan?”

“Right!”

Aihara and Colin exchanged a smile and a glance. It seemed they had grown pretty close while I wasn’t paying attention. This must be what they call a “social powerhouse.”

…But still, is it really possible to learn to speak, even if it’s broken, in just half a day just because you’re good at communication? Wait, could it be that Aihara is actually quite talented?

As I was amazed by Aihara’s potential, she clasped her hands in front of me, striking a pleading pose.

“Hey, hey, Senpai. Holly-san said it’s okay, so can we stay at the castle? Please?”

“Uh, yeah, if that’s the case, I guess we can take her up on her offer. Umm, Holly-san, could you look after Aihara for the night?”

“Of course, leave it to me.”

Holly nodded reassuringly. I felt a bit pushed by Aihara’s overwhelming social skills, but I could relax knowing Holly would handle things.

“Thank you. Well, I have to go now because someone’s waiting for me. …Aihara, try not to cause too much trouble, okay?”

“‘Try not to’!? Doesn’t that already assume I’m going to be a bother!? Don’t worry, Senpai! See you tomorrow!”

With Aihara waving energetically, I headed back to the fortress once again.

+++

# 206. A House Visit 2

While dodging Maristel’s protests of “You’re so late!”, we continued climbing up the slope. 

Incidentally, it seemed like Isezaki had figured out that I had gone to contact the castle. Impressive, as always.

Eventually, we reached the highest point of the fortress. There stood an impressive watchtower. A little further away, a small stone house stood alone. It seemed this was Maristel’s home.

“We’re here! This is my hoooouse! Come on in, don’t be shy!”  

Maristel enthusiastically pushed us from behind, and both Isezaki and I stumbled into her house.

With a loud *bang*, the door closed, cutting off the light from outside, making the interior even dimmer. In the center of the room stood a large table with chairs around it. There were doors leading to other rooms to the front and left.

Along the walls were a small magic stove and kitchen utensils, though it didn’t look like they had ever been used. The shelves next to the stove had a few dishes but were mostly empty.

The whole place was plain and devoid of any sense of living. It reminded me of those minimalist rooms I’d seen on TV. That was my first impression of Maristel’s house.

Considering Maristel’s flashy and careless personality, I had expected a messy, cluttered room with no space to walk. Instead, I felt relieved, though also slightly let down. It was a strange feeling.

“Still… how should I put it? It’s very… neat? Organized?” 

I tried to offer some comment on the room, carefully choosing my words. Maristel raised an eyebrow and grinned.

“Hehe? What’s that, Matsunaga? You don’t have to sugarcoat it, you know. You can just say it’s an empty room! I’ve never settled in one place before, so I’m used to only having the bare minimum of things, ready to move at any time.”

It seemed this was Maristel’s default lifestyle. Thankfully, she didn’t seem offended by my comment.

“And I’m not even allowed to keep my cute living dead dolls here. They would have made things so lively.”

Being greeted by zombies at the door? No, thank you.

“I’ll turn on the lights.” 

Maristel murmured, snapping her fingers.

Suddenly, with a low *pop pop pop*, pale blue flames appeared along the walls.

“Uh… this is really creepy…”

The flames, when you looked closely, resembled human faces. And if you listened hard enough, you could hear faint, eerie voices like “Oooooooooh…”

This was definitely some kind of ghostly fire. The brightness was nice, but the atmosphere had become overwhelmingly eerie.

“Um, Maristel, honestly, I think the darkness was better than this…”

“Oh? That’s a cute thing to say” 

Maristel giggled, snapping her fingers again. The ghostly flames vanished instantly, and she quickly pressed a switch on the wall.

This time, a soft artificial light flickered on from a magic lamp hanging from the ceiling.

“Better now, right? I prefer the other light, but I’ll cater to my guests.”

“Uh, yeah… thanks. By the way, those ghost fires—were those also part of your magic? I’ve heard complaints about you walking around with them before.”

“Yep, those were mine. Necromancy isn’t just about turning dead bodies into dolls, you know that, right?”

“Ah, right… now that you mention it, you did summon a huge ghost before, didn’t you? What was it called, an Eldritch? Isezaki took it down so fast that I completely forgot about it.”

“You didn’t have to remind me of that, Matsunaga… That was one of my trump cards! You have no idea how much effort it took to summon it…” 

Maristel grumbled, veins bulging on her temple as she shot a glare at Isezaki. Isezaki just stood there, proudly puffing out her chest.

“Oh, but if you can summon things other than living dead, couldn’t you have helped in the battle during the herb-gathering mission?”

“My dear, certain necromancy spells don’t work well in sunlight.” 

“Exactly. My little dolls have physical bodies, so they aren’t as affected, but spirits lose their strength in sunlight.”

Hmm, so there are all kinds of magic, huh? As usual, there’s so much I don’t understand about this other world. I want to know more details, but Isezaki-san doesn’t teach me too much. She says something like, “It’s not good to get bound by common sense”.

…And with that, Maristel clapped her hands together, and the dry sound echoed in the sterile room.

“Well, enough chatting. How about we eat? I’m actually starving, you know.”

“Ah, that sounds good.”

“I don’t have any objections.”

“Got it! You two wait here. I’ll go prepare everything now!”

Maristel gestured for me and Isezaki-san to sit, then headed toward the entrance. She went out of her way to invite us to her home, so I’m pretty curious about what she’s going to serve us…

“I’ll just go raid the pantry real quick~♪ I heard the soldiers around here hunted down some monsters that were messing up the area yesterday. They’ve probably already been butchered, so the meat should be perfect to eat right now—”

“Wait a minute.”

“Gah!”

I grabbed Maristel by the collar just as she was about to leave the house. Isezaki-san also looked at her with a mix of shock and exasperation.

“’Maristel… did you already forget how my husband sternly warned you earlier?”

At this, Maristel’s eyes darted around like she had genuinely just remembered.

“Ah—oh! Right, this is no good, is it?! But now… hmm, if that’s the case, the stalls outside must be closed, so I guess we’ll have to go to the canteen inside the fortress? But whenever I go there, I can’t relax with all the soldiers staring at me. Ugh, being too attractive has its downsides, you know~♪”

Maristel said this while sensually brushing her hair back, clearly enjoying the attention. However, from everything I’ve seen so far, I’m pretty sure the soldiers are just watching her to make sure she doesn’t cause any more trouble. But I’ll leave that unsaid for now.

That being said, I’m not too thrilled about eating while being stared at by soldiers either… Looks like I have no choice.

“Alright, I’ll handle the food today.”

“Oh? I feel a little bad, but what will our traveling merchant with that handy [Storage Space] whip up for us? Whatever you serve, I’ll happily gobble it up~♡”

For some reason, Maristel glanced at my crotch—but I ignored her and focused on thinking about the menu.

“Hmm, let’s see… Isezaki-san, is there anything you want to eat?”

“Ah! I’ll eat anything you make, husband! Anything’s fine! I’ll gobble it right up!”

Isezaki-san, her face bright red, also glanced at my crotch, competing with Maristel. This isn’t helping me decide. Also, I really wish they’d stop staring down there—it’s embarrassing.

Alright, what should I take out from my [Storage Space]? I turned my back on them to hide myself while I thought about it.

But… I originally came to this other world as part of Aihara’s sightseeing plan. And if it’s sightseeing, we should be eating local food. So I didn’t bring much with me in terms of meals.

In that case… I guess I have no choice. I feel bad for Isezaki-san, but…

With a heavy heart, I took out ‘that’. And then—

“Eh? Eh!? What is this? What is this!?”

Maristel’s eyes sparkled at the item I pulled from the [Storage Inventory].

+++

# 207. Rush! What's for Dinner at Your Place?

I handed Maristel a cup of instant noodles. I had bought a whole box of these during my journey to the capital, dreaming of eating them while enjoying the scenery. However, I got tired of them after just three days, and they ended up being stored away in my [Storage Space].

Maristel picked up the cup of noodles, her eyes gleaming with curiosity as she examined it from various angles.

“Wow, hmm, interesting… These are characters I don’t recognize… And the paper is soft yet transparent like glass… It feels so strange and crinkly… Kind of like the wings of a shell insect? So, humans make stuff like this, huh?”

“Y-Yeah, something like that. But it’s not widely available. I deal with particularly rare items even among humans. That’s how I was able to get an audience with Lady Levia.”

“Hmm, I always thought humans were all idiots, but there are monsters like you. So maybe they aren’t completely useless. So, how do you eat this? I mean, I get that you’re supposed to eat what’s inside.”

“Yes, here’s how you do it—”

I removed the outer film and peeled off the lid.

“Eh… You eat this hard thing? Isn’t it tougher than black bread?”

“There’s one more step to it.”

I took her hand away from poking the dry noodles suspiciously and poured hot water into the cup using an electric kettle from my [Storage Space].

“Oh, I see, you soak it in hot water!? It’s like dried meat—oh, it smells good! Hey, Matsunaga, can I eat it now?”

Maristel was about to peel off the lid we had just closed when Isezaki-san smacked her hand.

“Hold on, Maristel. Not yet. Count to 180. Or maybe waiting for around 500 would make it tastier…”

“Oh, Isezaki-san likes it a bit overcooked, huh? I prefer it slightly firmer. By the way, Isezaki-san, do you usually eat cup noodles?”

“Yes, occasionally. My grandmother says, ‘Rock needs some junky kick too,’ so…”

“I see…”

I could almost picture the landlady slurping down cup noodles with unusual gusto.

“Hey! I don’t care about your grandma! So, how long do I have to wait? I can’t wait for 500!”

Maristel was about to open the lid again when Isezaki-san grabbed her hand.

“Then let’s keep it simple and go with 180 this time.”

“Count to 180? Got it! One-three-four-five-six-seven-eight—”

◇◇◇

—And so, three minutes passed. She was counting a bit fast, but let’s not get picky.

“Is it ready now? Is it!? I’m eating it now, I can’t wait! Here I go!”

With that, Maristel peeled off the lid. She jabbed a fork into the cup, which she had grabbed from the shelf, and scooped up a big bite, shoving it into her mouth.

“Hot!”

“Well, of course, it’s hot… Here, have some tea.”

I brought her a ceramic cup from the shelf and poured in some ice-cold tea from a thermos I’d stored in my [Storage Space].

Maristel gulped it down in silence, then started blowing on the noodles to cool them. After a moment of caution, she took another bite, chewing it thoroughly. 

Suddenly, she sprang to her feet, shouting so loudly it echoed through the house.

“Delicious! Delicious! What is this!? It’s so, so, so gooood!”

Her cheeks flushed with bliss as she hugged herself tightly. Her almond-shaped eyes opened wide, glistening with excitement. If this were a cooking manga, her clothes would be coming off in a dramatic reveal.

“The noodles are smooth yet chewy when you bite into them, and the rich broth with its roasted aroma clings to them perfectly! The more I eat, the more I want! Ah, no! I’ve never had anything like this! This is amazing, too amazing! _Slurp, slurp, sluuurp_!”

Maristel, having expressed her thoughts on the meal, returned to her seat and continued to slurp the noodles with fervor. Well, it seems she liked them, so that’s a relief.

Watching Maristel with a satisfied nod, Isezaki-san turned to me with a smile.

“As expected of my husband’s cup ramen! Even Maristel is like this after eating it!”

“Uh, no, it’s just regular cup ramen… Sorry, but Isezaki-san, would you mind having cup ramen for dinner too?”

“Mind? Not at all. I’m happy with anything you prepare for me, husband. Oh, I know, I’ll try the noodles a bit firmer this time!”

Isezaki-san chuckled softly, narrowing her eyes in delight. She’s such a considerate girl, even to an old man like me who could only prepare cup noodles.

◇◇◇

So, a bit later, we prepared our own cups of ramen and started eating. By then, Maristel had already finished hers, down to the last drop of broth. As she returned from her state of culinary euphoria, she picked up the empty cup and began fiddling with it, speaking up once more.

“Hmm, no matter how many times I look at it, this container is just so fascinating. It’s waterproof, light, fragile, yet elastic… Hey, Matsunaga… Can I ask you for a favor? Could you give me this container?”

“Sure, no problem. Do you want the ones we used too? Just please don’t mention where they came from, alright? It’s part of my business secret.”

“Of course! I would never do anything that would hurt you, Matsunaga! Thank you, Matsunaga, love you, muah muah muah~♡”

Maristel blew a series of kisses my way, but Isezaki-san cut in, leaning forward and glaring at Maristel.

“Don’t worry, Husband. The [Sacred Oath] is in effect. Maristel cannot do anything that would harm you.”

“Oh, Isezaki, don’t be so tactless. Even without any collar, I’m on Matsunaga’s side~.”

“Hmph, we’ll see about that.”

Isezaki-san turned away with a huff. Maristel watched her with a look of amusement, replying with a smirk.

“Anyway, I was supposed to treat you, but you ended up treating me instead, and I got something nice too… I do feel a bit guilty. Maybe I should repay you with my body—”

Before she could finish, Isezaki-san turned back, glaring sharply at Maristel, who shrugged.

“…But that’s something for the future. For now, I want to give you something in return. So… how about this? You came here to make potions, right? I know a bit about alchemy myself and could lend you a hand. Why don’t you come and make them in the other room?”

Maristel pointed to the room next door.

“There’s a basement over there that serves as my lab. It’s equipped with all sorts of equipment, so it should be helpful for making potions.”

“That sounds great. We’d appreciate the help!”
