As I tried to leave in a hurry, the landlady grabbed my arm tightly. 

“What are you saying! A banquet like this without Matsunaga-kun? No way! Let’s enjoy this dark dinner together!” 

Once it gets to this point, I can’t stop the landlady. 

I immediately looked to Isezaki-san for help. But she just met my eyes and shook her head weakly. 

And so, I was forcibly roped into the banquet of darkness.

◇◇◇

“YEAHHH! Grilled whole Shadow Bat is the best! There’s still more! Come on, Matsunaga-kun, eat too!” 

With a big grin, the landlady took a huge bite out of the grilled Shadow Bat. She then pushed the plate towards me. 

For some reason, the Shadow Bat on the plate was standing upright with its wings spread,. It was glaring at me like it was about to attack. 

Anyone who could eat with that kind of sight must be crazy.

“Uh, no, since it’s special, please enjoy it yourself, Landlady…” 

“Really? You don’t have to hold back. Colin, you’ll eat it, right?” 

“Can I!? Then I’ll dig in!” 

Colin bit into the bat’s head just like the landlady. 

“_*Chomp chomp*_… It’s delicious!” 

Colin grinned widely while gripping the Shadow Bat’s torso. 

Seeing that, the landlady nodded in satisfaction. 

“Yeah, yeah. Great appetite, Colin! Seina, you too, eat up!” 

“I-I’m fine with just the fried pieces like Uncle’s…” 

Saying that, Isezaki-san took a bite of the fried Shadow Bat. 

The karaage (fried dish) made from the bat’s br3ast meat was the only dish that could be considered edible here. 

But even though it used br3ast meat, it was strangely crunchy. It was giving it an odd texture. 

It wasn’t bad per se, but… like, cartilage from chicken already covers that need, you know?

By the way, according to the landlady, the skull is crispy like a corn snack. And the wings are crunchy like potato chips. 

“Seina, you’re too reserved. Hey Colin, should the two of us finish this off?” 

“Yes, Granny!”

And the two of them eagerly chomped down on more Shadow Bat. 

Just watching that was enough to make my stomach feel heavy. 

So I took out my smartphone from my pocket.

“Landlady, do you mind if I show this meal scene to Aihara too?” 

“Of course not! But if Rio gets jealous later, just know there’s no ingredients left!” 

I see, so no ingredients left. That means this dark banquet ends tonight. 

Feeling secretly relieved, I replied.

“Yes, I just want Aihara to get a sense of the atmosphere here… Okay, cheese.” 

“YEEEAAHH!” 

At the moment the landlady bit into the Shadow Bat’s head and stuck up her middle finger, I snapped the photo. 

I then sent it to Aihara via LANE.

This was just a little harassment toward Aihara, who wasn’t present. But thinking that someone else was going through the same thing made me feel a bit lighter. 

Sorry, Aihara. Thank you, Aihara. 

And so, I somehow managed to survive the rest of the banquet. 

—But as I was about to leave, the landlady unusually came to see me off at the entrance. She said one thing: 

“Thank you so much for today, Matsunaga-kun! If there’s ever a chance, bring me another Shadow Bat, okay?” 

With a genuinely happy smile that resembled Isezaki-san’s a little, I couldn’t bring myself to say no. I could only nod vaguely.

+++

# 230. The Price of the Banquet

The day after the secret banquet at the Isezaki residence. 

A message from Aihara arrived on LANE.

“Heeeyyyyy Senpai~~!! Don’t send me pictures like that, seriously! I saw it right after waking up and thought my heart was gonna stop! If you send another one, I’m seriously gonna block you!!”

It came with a stamp of an angry rabbit.

Last night, I had thought she was taking a long time to read the message. But apparently, Aihara had fallen asleep early. 

If she saw *that* right after waking up, then yeah, I guess I do feel a little bad.

“My bad. I wasn’t myself yesterday. Let me make it up to you by treating you to a meal sometime. Please forgive me.”

Right after I sent that message, a reply came back.

“For real!? Then I’ll specially forgive you! Anyway, I’m heading off to work now! Looking forward to dinner~♡”

This time, the stamp showed a rabbit making a heart with its ears. 

Looks like she forgave me.

It’s nice that she’s easygoing. But now the “meal” has been upgraded to “dinner,” and that’s a bit worrying. 

I might need to lay down some boundaries early so she doesn’t drag me to a super fancy place.

“Alright then…”

I put my phone away and headed to the Isezaki residence. 

As usual, I took Colin with me to take care of today’s errands. 

By the way, Isezaki-san had school today and wasn’t home.

First up: deliver the monster meat to Mr. Juuzou—

And so, Colin and I used **[Dimensional Teleport]** to jump to Mr. Juuzou’s hospital room. 

We handed over the usual monster meat and received the reward: 100,000 yen.

According to Mr. Juuzou, recently, he and Aihara have been enjoying something like “at-home yakiniku”. But instead it’s become “hospital-room yakiniku,” once a week. 

Hospital yakiniku… is that really okay? 

But I guess common sense doesn’t apply to VIPs.

Usually, he would happily take the meat while thinking about grilling it with his granddaughter. But today, Mr. Juuzou seemed oddly off. 

He held the package as far from his body as possible and even avoided looking at it.

“Um… Mr. Juuzou, is something wrong?”

“It’s nothing… N-no, actually, I should double-check. Just to be sure—this is the usual wild boar meat, right?”

“Huh? Of course it is…”

“I-I see. That’s good then. Sorry, Matsunaga-kun. A-ah, also, could you tell my sister-in-law to maybe go easy on the weird stuff…”

Judging by his strained smile, it seems Mr. Juuzou also saw *that* photo via Aihara.

I mean, I’m the one who took the picture. So maybe I shouldn’t say this. But yeah… that image does leave a strong impression. 

Looks like I gave Mr. Juuzou a new trauma he didn’t need.

Feeling super guilty, I left the hospital room and headed to Mr. Shouda’s room next. 

I was hoping we could also talk a bit about potion sales while I was at it.

But on the way there, I heard lively voices coming from the courtyard. 

I looked over and saw Mr. Shouda surrounded by several elderly people.

It seems Mr. Shouda is quite the ladies’ man—he was happily chatting away with a group of VIP-looking older women around his age.

Since he seemed to be in the middle of having fun, I thought about turning back for now— 

But right then, Mr. Shouda met my gaze and waved me over.

No choice, so Colin and I headed into the courtyard.

“Oh my, and who might this young man be?”

The women looked at us with curiosity.

“Yes, this is a friend of mine. And this little one is his niece. Looks like they came to visit today.”

“I’m Koutarou Matsunaga.”

“I’m Colin!”

“Oh my, how wonderful to have such a young friend come visit. I’m jealous. When my kids or grandkids come, it’s always just to talk about money or business.”

“It’s the same for me. They only see me as a wallet.”

“You’re lucky. Lately, all I get are talks about my will. It really brings me down. I’m starting to think I should just talk to my lawyer and donate everything somewhere.”

“If that’s how it is, wouldn’t it be better to find a nice man now and give it all to him?”

“Oh my, you naughty lady!” 

“Oh come on now!” 

“Oh ho ho ho ho ho ho!”

Seems that whether they’re VIPs or neighborhood aunties, ladies are the same everywhere. 

Before I knew it, they were deep into gossip and completely forgot about us.

Seeing that, Mr. Shouda gave a wry smile and spoke.

“Well then, everyone, I’ll take my leave around here.”

“Yeees, Mr. Shouda. Let’s chat again sometime!”

And so, we entered Mr. Shouda’s hospital room. As soon as we stepped inside, Mr. Shouda sank into the sofa. He was completely worn out.

“Good grief, I’m really tired.”

“Haha… Mr. Shouda, you’re really popular, huh.”

His eyes are narrow, but his facial features are well-shaped. And he has a sharp look. He must’ve been quite popular in his younger days.

But in response to my words, Mr. Shouda shrugged as he lit a cigarette.

“Good grief, what a cruel irony. I’m doing it for your sake, you know.”

“Huh? What do you mean?”

“My social circle in this hospital ward isn’t very wide. Embarrassingly enough, my daily routine used to be walking around the courtyard with unsteady steps without talking to anyone, and killing time sitting on a bench. …But for those who remember how I used to be, they must be curious, thinking, ‘That old man’s gotten quite lively,’ right?”

“That’s true.”

The first time I saw Mr. Shouda, he was just sitting on a bench. He was not moving—like you couldn’t tell if he was asleep, awake, or maybe even dead. But now he walks around energetically and even smokes with ease.

“Right now, I’m fishing in those people who speak to me out of curiosity and investigating them bit by bit. Whether they have some bodily issue they’re desperate enough to need a miracle for, whether they can afford the cost for it, whether they can keep a secret—that sort of thing. Maybe I’m being a bit too laid-back? If you really need money right now, we can shorten the process. I could even lend you some if you’d like.”

“Ah, no. I’m satisfied with what I’ve received from you, Mr. Shouda. So please, take your time to search.”

I’ve got enough money. And even if I didn’t, I wouldn’t want to borrow any. Owing this person something is kind of scary. Whether he knows that or not, Mr. Shouda nodded with satisfaction.

“Understood. I’ll take my time and find a patient who matches your needs. Look forward to it.”

Looks like he’s actually doing a more thorough search than I expected. Since his first impression was that “birthday surprise”, part of me was trying to test him. But maybe I can trust him after all.

After parting ways with Mr. Shouda, Colin and I next jumped to the other world. Today was the second day of supply transport.

According to Holly’s story from the other day, the supply transport will probably end this time or next. I’d like to finish things off swiftly again today without running into Maristel.

Wishing for that, I used **[Dimensional Teleport]** together with Colin to move to the other world.

+++

# 231. The Final Cargo

To transport the materials, Colin and I came to Lady Levia’s castle.

Then, guided by Holly, we arrived at the plaza. There, a large number of cargos filled with materials were already lined up. And Holly turned to face me in front of them.

“Matsunaga-sama, this will be the last material transport.”

“I see. So that means the reopening of the mine is finally in sight.”

“Exactly. The reason the project has proceeded so quickly up to this point is entirely thanks to your assistance, Matsunaga-sama. On behalf of Lady Levia, I offer you my heartfelt gratitude.”

Saying that, Holly bowed deeply. I waved my hand lightly.

“Oh no, it wasn’t that much trouble. So don’t worry about it. If anything comes up again, feel free to ask me anytime.”

But to that light comment, Holly’s eyes glinted sharply.

“Then, if I may be direct, I have a request.”

“Wh-What is it…?”

Ignoring me as I tensed up at the sudden request, Holly quietly opened her mouth.

“Twelve days from now, we will hold a ceremony outside of Magic Fortress Maristel to celebrate the redevelopment of the magic stone mine. This ceremony will be very important. As it will serve to show both within and outside the territory that the reclamation and redevelopment of the mine were Lady Levia’s achievements.”

I see. Since she plans to petition the king for the independence of Levia’s domain based on the success of the mine’s reopening, a flashy appeal would certainly be necessary.

“At that ceremony, Matsunaga-sama, we would like you to attend as Lady Levia’s right hand—”

“I refuse.”

I immediately refused. I don’t need unnecessary fame. And I **absolutely** don’t want to stand out. However, as if she already knew how I would respond, Holly continued speaking without flinching.

“Understood. Then at least, would you consider watching over Lady Levia at the ceremony alongside Isezaki-sama? Lady Levia also strongly wishes for your attendance.”

“Ah, in that case, I’d be happy to.”

To Isezaki-san, it’s an important moment for her dear little sister. I’m sure she’d want to see it. And I’d like to enjoy the ceremony too—as a spectator.

“Thank you very much. And, one more thing… I have a personal request. On the day of the ceremony, could you use **[Dimensional Teleport]** to transport Lady Levia from Grandain to the magic stone mine? By shortening the travel time, we hope to give Lady Levia, who is burdened with heavy responsibilities, at least a bit of rest.”

The seriousness in Holly’s expression deepened. It seems this was her main request all along. Of course, if it’s just that, it’s no big deal.

“Sure, that much is no problem.”

At my answer, Holly finally relaxed her expression.

“Thank you very much. Then we’ll proceed with that plan. …Since this is a personal favor from me, as a reward, I offer you my body—”

“_*AHEM!!*_ That much I’ll do for free!!”

“Oh…I thought my body is at least attractive—”

Holly slumped her shoulders in disappointment.

“_*COUGH COUGH!*_ No, that’s not what I meant! _*AHEM!*_ Well, now that we’ve finished talking, I’ll get to work on the cargo!”

Even though Colin is right next to her, what is this sister saying? While coughing repeatedly, I awkwardly headed over to start collecting the cargo.

—

While Holly and Colin began exchanging information about our stay in Japan out of the corner of my eye, I stored the cargos gathered in the plaza into my **[Storage Space]**.

—And so, the job was over in no time. **[Storage Space]** really is the ultimate magic when it comes to transporting goods.

With that, half the job was done. All that remained was to deliver the materials to the frontline base.

So, just like last time, I thought I’d let Holly and Colin enjoy some sister-only time.

I subtly put some distance between us and tried to activate **[Dimensional Teleport]** alone—at that moment.

“Colin, don’t let him escape!”

“Yes, Big Sis!”

The sisters shouted sharply. Looks like my attempt was completely seen through.

But there was enough distance between me and them. I should be able to get away—was what I thought for just a moment.

Colin lowered her stance. She then kicked off the ground with a force that gouged into the earth.

**_——CRACK!_**

A sound like the ground bursting echoed. Colin then charged at me with the speed of a bullet. That force was nothing compared to last time. In the blink of an eye, she closed the distance. And before I knew it, she was right in front of me.

Ah, I might die.

The image of Colin, with all that momentum, piercing through my stomach flashed through my mind. The very next moment, as I was sensing death approaching—

Colin came to an abrupt stop right in front of me. Her movement ignored the very laws of inertia. And I unconsciously held my breath in awe.

Then, she swiftly grabbed my hand like she was snatching it—and the two of us **[Dimensional Teleport]** to the wilderness near the magic stone mine.

◇◇◇

“Matsunaga-sama! It is unacceptable to leave behind your bodyguard!”

“Y-Yeah. Sorry, I won’t do it again…”

As soon as we arrived in the wilderness, Colin puffed out her cheeks and scolded me angrily. I honestly apologized. It seems like the last time she let it slide. But going without an escort again wasn’t going to be allowed.

Well, I mean, yeah. If it gets to the point where I feel like I might die, it’s better not to overthink things. I nearly ended up like Demon King Picc◯l◯ getting done in by Gok◯ or something.

With heartfelt relief, I took Colin along and headed toward the frontline base where Captain Beard was waiting.

—

As we walked at the foot of the magic stone mine, we looked around at the state of urban development in the surrounding area.

Once the magic stone mine reopens, this region will not only produce magic stones and other minerals. But people will also gather here for various reasons—such as the natural resources that had long been untouched due to years of conflict, and the wild animals and monsters that can be hunted and sold for high prices. The economy is bound to rapidly develop.

This hopeful town was changing its appearance at a rapid pace.

Until very recently, this entire area had been crowded with tents and stalls—lively but messy. Now, well-maintained roads stretched out. And solid stone buildings had begun to line both sides. The change was simply astonishing.

As we walked further, I spotted a short, stocky man among the workers doing construction. He was producing perfectly-shaped blocks of stone from thin air.

It was probably magic. I’d seen magic that created stone spears and earthen arrows before. This was likely a similar kind of applied magic.

There were also a few workers using magic to produce mud-like material. They used it to repair roads and building exteriors.

Holly had mentioned that earth magic technicians had only just arrived recently—these must be them.

With the help of earth magic technicians, buildings and roads can apparently be constructed many times faster than usual. Magical construction is seriously amazing.

We continued walking and taking in the lively streetscape. Finally, we arrived at the frontline base and went to visit Captain Beard.

+++

# 232. Interception Preparations

“Welcome, Matsunaga-sama!”

“Captain Bea—no, I mean Captain Higuner, thank you. I heard this is the last material transport… The room feels quite empty now.”

I glanced around the command room of the frontline base as I spoke.

I remember that the shelves used to be stuffed with thick books and old parchments. And the desk was cluttered with maps and writing tools.

Now, the shelves were completely empty. There wasn’t a desk or chair in sight. The faint markings on the wall might be where a heraldic flag was taken down. It looked like someone was about to flee in the middle of the night.

“Yes, actually, we’ve already moved operations to the magic fortress. So we hardly use this place anymore,” 

Captain Beard said. He was also surveying the room.

Now that he mentioned it, this base had indeed been a *frontline* base during conflicts. But with the construction of the magic fortress, it was no longer near the front. And it had likely lost its strategic value.

“Therefore, this base will be dismantled as soon as the materials you’ve brought are used up.”

“I see, that makes sense. In that case—”

I couldn’t stay for small talk. I quickly urged Captain Beard to lead me to the warehouse.

Last time, we were lucky Maristel didn’t show up. But there’s no guarantee she won’t this time. Better to finish things before any trouble starts—but…

Unfortunately, I heard the sharp **_*clack clack clack*_** of heels on stone pavement from outside the room.

With a small sigh, I began preparing to intercept.

Last time, when Maristel suddenly tried to hug me, I reflexively used [Eject]. But I felt a bit bad about it afterward. So this time, I’d block her with a spatial barrier.

As I focused my mind to summon a dimensional wall at any moment, I watched the door. I held my breath—

**_*BANG!*_** The door burst open violently.

“Yah~n! Matsunaga! It’s been so long~~~!!”

It **was** Maristel. Dressed in her usual provocative gown, she threw her arms wide and leapt toward me as soon as she saw me.

Her bountiful chest loomed closer—but I was ready this time.

Just as I prepared to summon the barrier, a small figure jumped between us. It was Colin.

With her back to me, she threw her head back dramatically. She then launched forward with a sharp snap.

“HMPH!!”

A full-on headbutt. Colin’s small, hard-looking head smashed into Maristel’s soft-looking belly in a perfect counterattack.

“GUWAAAAAAAHHHHHHHHH!!”

Pitifully, Maristel was blown away and slammed into the stone wall—

**_*CRAAAAAAAAAASH!!*_**

The impact was loud enough to shake the entire stone building.

Outside, the soldiers stirred.

“Are we under attack!?”

“Send a messenger!”

“Wait! I saw Maristel go in just now.”

“Oh, then it’s fine?”

“Yeah…”

“Cancel the alert! Cancel the alert!”

I felt a strange sadness at how accustomed the soldiers were to Maristel-related chaos.

Meanwhile, Maristel was still slumped against the wall, not moving.

…Huh? When I hit her with [Eject], she got back up pretty quickly. Could it be that Colin’s headbutt is even stronger than [Eject]?

Actually, if Colin hadn’t stepped in, I might’ve taken that hit myself… A cold sweat ran down my back as I nervously turned to Colin.

“C-Colin-chan… Maristel is still technically an ally… so, maybe go a little easier next time?”

“I was given strict orders from Lady Isezaki to never let Maristel get close!”

“I-I see…”

So Isezaki-san had predicted this scenario and asked Corinne to intervene.

I knew she hated it when Maristel clung to me. Maybe this was her way of showing jealousy… which, honestly, was kind of cute?

Still, Maristel looked seriously out of it. I cautiously approached and looked at her face.

She was completely white-eyed and twitching uncontrollably.

…Ah, this is bad.

I quickly took a potion out of my [Storage Space] and poured it over her.

A gentle light wrapped around her. It gradually healed her. Eventually, her eyes regained focus. And she suddenly sprang to her feet.

“Hey, you little brat! I saw my dead grandma waving at me across a river! What the hell was that for!?”

“I will not tolerate any insolence toward Matsunaga-sama! On behalf of Lady Isezaki, I will defend him! Hmph!”

Colin puffed out her chest proudly. But Maristel only looked around, smirked, and said—

“Oh? Oh ho ho ho? Isezaki isn’t here today? Ohhh, I see how it is~”

Her belligerent tone vanished. She pranced up to me with a twinkle in her eye.

“In that case~ Matsunaga~ Why don’t we let the little one stay behind, and the two of us have some quality alone time? You’re free today, right? Let’s take it nice and slow together~”

As she pressed her chest toward me, I quickly stepped away.

“No, thank you. I have a beloved wife.”

As always, I used Isezaki-san as a human shield. I wasn’t about to let a moment of weakness drag me into trouble.

Maristel pouted and protested loudly.

“Aww, come onnn! You’re always so cold! …But I don’t hate that about you either ♡ Hey hey, if I just ‘accompany’ you on your work, that’s okay, right? Pretty please? I was such a good girl and followed your orders and everything~”

Wiggling her body and clinging to me, she begged.

Ignoring her, I turned to Captain Beard and shot him a look that asked, “Was she really being good?”

He nodded.

“Actually, she was bedridden with a cold until recently. After recovering, she’s been calmer and causing fewer problems.”

“Exactly! I was _so_ sick! And Beard, seriously—if you thought something was wrong, you could’ve at least come check on me!”

“Who would’ve thought a demon could catch a cold!? You’re always going on about how demons are beautiful, wise, and strong!”

“That kind of fragile side is part of my charm, okay? Honestly, Beard, you really don’t understand women at all~”

“I—I do understand women very well!”

“Oh really~? I know you tried to hit on your secretary and got rejected~ Then you went on a three-day drinking binge with your subordinates, didn’t you~?”

“W-What!? How do you know about that!?”

“Hmm~ Who knows~”

And just like that, Captain Beard and Maristel were bickering.

I was a little curious about his romance drama with the secretary. But the key point was: the reason Maristel wasn’t around last time was because she was sick.

And apparently, since recovering, she’d been better behaved—maybe not perfect, but definitely improved.

In that case, maybe I could grant her this small request. Letting her build up good behavior might help her eventually become a real proper demon.

As Maristel continued teasing Captain Beard, I said to her:

“Alright. If it’s just tagging along with my work, that’s fine. But the moment you get in the way, I’m sending you back.”

“Got it~! Come on, Matsunaga, let’s go~ ♪”

Maristel cheerfully walked beside me. Behind her, Colin followed with a wary eye. Leading us was Captain Beard, his face beet red from having his embarrassing past exposed.

And so, the whole group headed toward the warehouse, trailing along one after another.

+++

# 233. The Way Home

Using [Storage Space] to transport materials makes storing them easy. But taking them out is a bit of a hassle.

Since a large amount of materials can’t fit in a single room. Another reason is because the wooden boxes containing weapons, armor, food, building materials, and other categories must be somewhat organized when placed. Otherwise, the people who take them out later will have a hard time.

“Alright… there. Whew, that’s the last of it.”

Just as I finished such work and placed the last wooden box in the corner of the room, Maristel raised her voice as if impressed.

“Amaaaazing! Matsunaga, you always unload this much at once? That’s no good, y’know. Hoarding too much is bad for your body~. You should let it out regularly, okay?”

That… sounded kind of erotic. But maybe it’s just my imagination.

“I always transport about this much at once. Though this is the last time.”

“Huh~. They say the size of the [Storage Space] scales with mana capacity. But if it’s *this* big, then of course your mana smells this good.”

While saying that, Maristel brought her nose close to my neck and sniffed.

Among the demonfolk, Maristel possesses the special ability to smell mana. But honestly, from my side, I’d really rather she didn’t. Sniffing people for their smell is the act of a pervert. I subtly put distance between us.

“Ehh~? Can’t you at least let me smell you a little~? Stingy~”

“No way… Anyway, I’m done with my work here. So I’ll be heading back. I think I’ll come by again during Lady Levia’s ceremony. I’d appreciate your help again then.”

“Ha! Matsunaga-dono, good work!”

“Yup, good work~♡”

Captain Beard saluted, and Maristel waved her hand lightly. I turned my back to the two and left the frontline base with Colin.

◇◇◇

On the way back, just like when we came, I planned to use [Dimensional Teleport] behind the big boulder at the edge of town.

To get there, I walked through the developing townscape once more. Along the way, I suddenly noticed something and muttered aloud.

“The workers using earth magic… they’re all short and stocky…”

“Well, duh? They’re dwarves~”

“Huh, dwarves?”

“Earth magic means dwarves, right~? You didn’t know that, Matsunaga? You really are kind of clueless sometimes. But that part of you is adorable too♡”

So there are dwarves in this world too, not just demonfolk. Which means maybe there are those kinds of races and those kinds too.

Isezaki-san doesn’t really tell me much about this sort of thing. Well, at my age, surprises that feel truly fresh are rare. And I’m not trying to force the information out of her anyway.

…More importantly—

“Um, Maristel-san. How long are you going to keep following us?”

Even though we said goodbye at the frontline base, Maristel was following us like it was the most natural thing.

“Well, I mean~. We haven’t seen each other in so long~. Parting right away would be boring~”

My plan was to report to Holly, then visit the Reymar Trading Company. I wanted to start selling the products I bulk-bought at the 100-yen shop soon.

So I’d really like to part ways with Maristel around here. But she just wouldn’t leave.

“At least let me see you off to the carriage. I adjust the dolls at night, so I’m totally free right now. That much is fine, right~?”

Apparently, Maristel wanted to see us off until we left town. She probably just didn’t want to part ways so soon. That pure sentiment pricked at my conscience.

Still, it would be a problem if she kept following us. We weren’t using a carriage in the first place.

Now then, what to do… And maybe sensing the mood, Colin whispered to me:

“Matsunaga-sama, if you wish, I can render Maristel-san unconscious.”

In the next moment, Colin’s figure flickered and appeared behind Maristel. She raised her hand in a practiced stance.

If I just nodded, she would probably do *that* technique—the tap to the neck that knocks people out.

I’ve heard that doesn’t actually work. But if it’s Colin, she might really pull it off. No doubt.

“Hey, hey! Aren’t you two saying something dangerous?! Did I say something that weird!?”

Maristel flailed. She was startled by Colin’s sudden appearance behind her.

Well, she’s probably kind of an out-of-place character at the fortress. And I can kind of understand her feeling lonely when I leave.

Last time I left without saying anything, and I was the one who forcibly got her the job at the fortress. So I can’t help but feel some responsibility. What should I do…

While thinking about that, before I knew it, I had reached the big boulder at the edge of town—my destination.

Hmm… now that we’re here, maybe there’s no helping it anymore.

I turned around to Maristel with a bit of resignation. And for some reason, she was looking around the area with a lewd grin.

“Hehehe~! Oh my, Matsunaga~. Dragging me to a place this deserted… If you’re in the mood, just say so, okay? I’m always ready♡”

Maristel gleefully placed her hands on her dress straps. She looked like she was about to strip in an instant. So I quickly stopped her.

“No, wait, that’s not it. I just need to talk to you.”

“Eh? What is it? A love confession at this late hour? Matsunaga, you’re surprisingly romantic~”

“No, not that. But what I’m about to say—please keep it a secret, okay?”

“Mmhm, got it♡ You mean a secret relationship from Isezaki, right? Ufufu~ this is my first time~ So I’m super nervous~”

“I said that’s not it! Please, just calm down for a second.”

I’m already getting tired. I sighed and looked at the overly excited, completely misunderstanding Maristel.

Around her neck was a ‘Chikkawa’ necklace that looked way too cutesy for someone as sexy as her.

It had Isezaki-san’s custom magic [Sacred Oath] embedded in it. And apparently thanks to its effect, Maristel couldn’t betray me. …If that’s the case, maybe there’s no need to explain anything.

“Anyway! Just keep it a secret, okay?”

I confirmed it with Maristel, slightly fed up. Colin noticed my intent and looked up at me with slight surprise.

“Are you sure, Matsunaga-sama?”

“Yeah. Well, she’s got the necklace. Should be fine.”

“Understood! Then, in case anything happens, I’ll eliminate Maristel-san before she can speak. Leave it to me!”

“Wha—Eliminate?! What do you mean eliminate?! What’s going to happen to me now?! I’m seriously getting scared!”

Maristel’s face turned pale at Colin’s dangerous words.

She seemed to be totally misunderstanding something. But at this point, I might as well just get it over with before she starts complaining.

I grabbed Colin’s and Maristel’s hands.

“Eeep!”

Maristel jerked her hand away.

“Wh-Why are you touching me?! You always run away when I try to get close! And now you’re suddenly the one touching me—scary!”

Well, she’s not wrong. But explaining everything now is too much hassle.

I grabbed her hand again and, gripping it tightly, pulled her behind the rock.

“Uppiiiiiieeeee!”

Letting out a weird scream, Maristel cried with teary eyes.

“W-What are you going to do to me in a place like this?!”

I said nothing to the trembling Maristel and just spoke.

“[Dimensional Teleport].”

In that moment, our figures vanished from behind the big rock.

## 247

As Ichita and the others made their way towards the ruins of Pyroconia, they were attacked by numerous monsters but managed to repel them. The magic stones of the fallen monsters emitted a putrid stench, strengthening their belief that the source of the outbreak was in Pyroconia.

“This is the place.”

“Wow…”

“It’s just as we were told.”

Exiting the beast forest, they arrived in Pyroconia. As expected, the buildings were in ruins, overgrown with ivy and weeds and almost no traces of the demon inhabitants remained, eroded by time.

“It’s been a while since I’ve been here.”

“Yes, there’s no reason to come unless necessary.”

Returning to their homeland after a long time, Velvet and Gremilia felt a sense of emptiness and the passage of time, seeing that the place had deteriorated even more than before.

“Ah!”

“They’re here.”

“Kyu.”

“Gwooooooo!”

Scanning the area, they spotted monsters near a collapsed building. Noticing them, the monsters let out a roar and charged towards Ichita and the others.

“Hmph.”

“Ggyeee!”

Gremilia swung her hand, easily dispatching the attacking monster.

“Ggy!?”

“Gwa!”

“Gya gya!”

The roar of the monsters alerted other creatures, such as kobolds and hobgoblins, who then attacked Ichita and the others.

“Hmph.”

“Hah!”

“Kyu.”

“Gigyagaaa!”

Irithelis and the others easily defeated them. For Irithelis and her group, goblins and the like were no longer a challenge.

“Gwooo!”

“Kukkee!”

“Now it’s orcs and cockatrices, huh?”

More monsters, drawn by the sounds of the fallen goblins, attacked. Irithelis and the others swiftly dispatched them as well.

“This is endless!”

“Where are they all coming from? This is annoying!”

Gremilia grew increasingly irritated as the number of monsters seemed endless despite their efforts. The others shared her frustration, eager to resolve the situation. As they fought, Serotiate noticed the source of the monsters’ appearance. Ichita and the group moved towards it, fighting off monsters along the way.

“This is it… I think.”

“It looks like they’re coming from underground, near this building…”

“This place… wasn’t it…”

“A guild building… hmph.”

They found that the monsters were emerging from a stone staircase leading up from the basement of a collapsed wall. Remembering that a guild building once stood there, Ichita and the others descended the staircase, fighting off the monsters as they went.

“Ah!”

“T-that’s a… Dungeon?!”

Descending the staircase and following the path deeper, they discovered a cave that appeared to be a dungeon. Monsters began emerging from it, confirming their suspicion that it was indeed a dungeon.

“…I can’t believe a dungeon actually formed here…”

“Yeah…”

Velvet and Gremilia were shocked to find a dungeon in their homeland. They wondered what could have caused it to form.

“Probably due to a reaction between the magic essence and the materials.”

“Reaction? With the dragon veins?”

This was the site of the adventurer guild, which would have needed a storage facility for materials brought back by adventurers. Serotiate suggested that the dungeon might have formed due to a chemical reaction between the dragon veins and the materials. However, Satyrbell sought further explanation, as this alone didn’t fully make sense.

“The materials of monsters accumulate miasma over time.”

“Really…?”

“I never knew that…”

It’s understandable they didn’t know – usually, materials are processed and consumed soon after being acquired, so this doesn’t typically happen. The explanation given was that miasma builds up when materials are left untouched for decades or even centuries.

“So… during the war when the country fell, the materials stored in the vault were left untouched for years, allowing miasma to accumulate…”

“And it reacted with the magic essence, giving birth to the dungeon…”

“This seems to be the most likely explanation.”

The group was stunned by the shocking truth of the dungeon’s birth, a reality unknown to anyone until now.

“This is… an incredible discovery…”

“Yes… but this…”

“It’s something that should be sealed.”

“Why…?”

They shook their heads, indicating they wouldn’t report this groundbreaking discovery to the world.

“It could cause unprecedented chaos, you see.”

“Unprecedented… really?”

They agreed it was better not to reveal it, explaining that it could lead to immense and prolonged confusion.

“Intentionally creating a dungeon could potentially cause some trouble.”

“Like this stampede we’re dealing with now.”

“Oh…”

“If we can’t handle a stampede…”

“Humans could be attacked…”

“Worst case, they might be wiped out.”

If people realize they can create dungeons intentionally, some might try to do so for personal gain. This could lead to catastrophic events like stampedes, causing immense disaster.

Hearing this, the group paled.

“…Keeping quiet seems to be the right choice.”

” ” “Yeah.” ” “

Ichita and the others decided not to report how the dungeon was created, believing it was the best course of action.

“…Alright, let’s go then.”

“Let’s go!”

“Kyu!”

“By the way, they’ve been annoying me for a while now.”

“Let’s wrap this up quickly.”

Even as Ichita and the others were deeply engaged in conversation, monsters kept emerging from the dungeon and attacking. However, they casually dispatched them while continuing their discussion.

Then, Ichita and the group ventured into the dungeon to stop the stampede.

+++

## 248

“Wow…”

“Incredible numbers…”

“They keep coming without end.”

“It’s getting annoying.”

“Kyu!”

As they enter the dungeon, a vast stone cavern, waves of monsters approach from the direction of their advance. There are goblins, kobolds, bone rabbits, big frogs, orcs and more. Ichita and his group easily dispatch the oncoming monsters. Although materials drop at their feet, they do not bother to pick them up, choosing to press forward. Their priority this time is to solve the problem, not gather materials. Besides, the drops are mostly insignificant, so they decide to ignore them.

“Endless! Really!”

“True!”

The number of approaching monsters keeps increasing, but Irithelis and the others swiftly eliminate them. While disposing of them is no trouble, their sheer numbers are causing difficulties.

“Ichita!”

“Got it.”

BOOM!

“Gugigeeeee!”

Ichita sweeps away the attacking monsters with a magic bullet gun. The new attribute-infused magic bullet gun is too powerful and could destroy the cavern, so he uses the ordinary magic bullet gun he had been using until now.

“Let’s go all out!”

At Satyrbell’s signal, everyone runs. They decide to reach the depths before more monsters appear, as progressing slowly would only invite more attacks.

Ichita and the others continue running without stopping, even as more monsters attack and they proceed to the depths while defeating the monsters.

“…We’ve reached a wide area.”

“The deepest part of the first floor.”

After running for a while, they arrive at a spacious area and immediately realize it is the deepest part of the first floor. There is a staircase leading downwards at the back.

GAGONG!

“Gwooooooo!”

Part of the wall next to the staircase leading downwards rises and an area boss appears.

“Orc General.”

“This isn’t something that should appear on the first floor.”

The “Orc General” is a B-rank monster, one of the higher ranks among the orc species. Its appearance on the first floor immediately alerts them that this dungeon is not to be underestimated.

“Pugyaaaaaaaaa!”

“Ugh! This is going to be troublesome!”

The Orc General’s roar summons a large number of orcs. Seeing this, they make a grim face, realizing that while defeating them is no problem, the sheer number will take time.

THUDDING SOUND!

“Alright, that’s done. Let’s move on.”

Ichita quickly dispatches them with his magic bullet gun, as they can’t afford to waste time and don’t need to fight on the enemy’s turf.

“By the way, how do we stop a stampede?”

Ichita asks while descending the staircase, seeking a specific method to resolve the situation, as he hadn’t been told how.

“According to records, it stops when the dungeon boss is defeated.”

“Simple and straightforward.”

Realizing that their task is to clear the dungeon, they become determined to finish quickly.

“Ugh… it’s hot!”

“This is a volcanic area…”

Upon reaching the second floor, they find themselves in a scorching volcanic region with magma erupting, an extremely challenging area. The moment they arrive, they wince from the heat, far more intense than a desert. Fortunately, Satyrbell quickly casts a barrier to mitigate the heat.

“Phew… what’s that?”

“They’ve arrived.”

“Next up, these guys.”

Hellhounds appear before Ichita and the others. Other monsters, such as Flame Lizards and Gargoyles, quickly attack as soon as they spot them.

“Let’s take them out quickly!”

“Let’s get out of here fast!”

Satyrbell uses a wide-area wind spell, slicing and dispatching the monsters and then they immediately rush forward. Although the barrier is protecting them from the heat, it doesn’t completely block it. So, they run again to escape this volcanic area.

“Ah! A Red Diamond!”

“Come on, let’s go!”

“Wait, I want that!”

As they run, a gem falls from the monsters they defeated and Velvet covets it. However, they are focused on escaping this area, so she is grabbed by the scruff of her neck and dragged along by Gremilia. Velvet cries, unable to obtain the treasure right before her eyes.

BOOM!

“Golem?”

“It’s not just a Golem! It’s a Lava Golem!”

As they continued running and reached a wide area, monsters rained down from above. It seemed that the area boss of the second floor was this Golem. Its black body resembled solidified lava, with rock seams and eyes glowing red like magma.

“Ow, it’s hot! It’s spitting fire!”

“Be careful. This Golem uses fire magic!”

As they threw a punch, fire erupted from its fist. It was a sudden attack, but Ichita and the others quickly dodged it.

“Ichita-sama!”

“Ow!”

The Lava Golem continued to spit fire without rest. Satyrbell dodged the attacks. While Satyrbell and the others were leading the Lava Golem, Ichita aimed and fired his magic gun, hitting the target. The Lava Golem’s upper body exploded and its unstable lower half collapsed, turning into particles and vanishing.

“Phew, let’s go!”

“Hurry up and get down!”

“Kyu!”

Despite successfully defeating the Lava Golem, they didn’t celebrate. Everyone was hot and wanted to leave the area quickly. That’s why they paid no attention to the items dropped by the Lava Golem and headed straight for the staircase leading deeper.

+++

## 249

“Brr! It’s cold!”

“Is this an ice and snow area?”

“Kyu kyu kyu!”

After defeating the Lava Golem, the area boss of the second floor and arriving at the third floor, they were immediately hit by a wave of cold. Looking around, everything was white and they couldn’t see more than a few meters ahead. Snow was falling heavily and the ground was covered in a thick layer.

Carbuncle clung to Ichita’s chest due to the intense cold. Ichita wrapped his hands around Carbuncle.

“This is tough…”

“Well, that’s something…”

The drastic temperature change put a significant strain on Ichita and the others. Additionally, the deep snow made movement difficult. Seeing this, Ichita took action.

“Then… it’s time for this!”

“Oh… the fire magic crystal!”

Ichita decided to use the newly crafted magic gun to break through the situation. Everyone understood his intention.

Ichita set the revolver with the fire magic crystal and aimed it forward, pulling the trigger.

Boom!

“Wow!”

“This is good!”

The fireball flew straight, evaporating the piled snow, creating a path. Additionally, the heat from the shots warmed the area and Ichita fired fire bullets around, blowing away the snow.

“Moving has become easier.”

“Thank you, Ichita-sama!”

“And the cold has eased quite a bit.”

With the snow cleared, movement became easier and the reduction in cold was a bonus.

“Look, a magic stone is falling.”

“Materials too.”

“Useful.”

It seemed that the gunshots had taken down nearby monsters. Hidden by the snow, they hadn’t noticed them, but by chance, defeating them made advancing easier. It was a three-birds-with-one-stone situation.

“Ah!”

“What’s wrong?”

“I found some fur, so I picked it up.”

During the move, the white fur was in a spot where it could be easily picked up. Upon examining it, it was an excellent material that didn’t let any cold through.

“This is really warm!”

“What kind of monster could this be?”

Since Ichita accidentally defeated it, they weren’t sure what kind of monster it was, but it was good material, so they decided to use it as is. They picked up enough fur for everyone and wrapped it around their upper bodies to ease the cold.

“We’ve arrived.”

“Thanks to you, Ichita-sama.”

After that, there were few monster attacks. It seemed that Ichita had mostly cleared the way, allowing them to easily reach the boss area. This boss area was surrounded by cliffs.

“Watch out, avoid it!”

“Whoa!”

“Was that…? A breath attack!”

Suddenly, they were attacked, but Satyrbell quickly noticed, allowing them to avoid it safely.

“It’s above us!”

Roar!

“Ice Dragon?”

Looking up at the cliff, a large shadow was seen. As the heavy snowfall weakened, the figure gradually became visible, revealing its identity. The one that had attacked Ichita and the others earlier was this Ice Dragon.

Rustle!

“Wait… was this blizzard caused by this dragon?”

As the Ice Dragon flapped its wings, a blizzard erupted, assaulting Ichita and the others. They shielded their faces against the fierce wind and focused on their target. Observing how the dragon manipulated the snow effortlessly, they realized this was the cause of the snow in this area.

Roar!

The Ice Dragon opened its mouth and launched an attack at Ichita and the others. They dodged just in time, watching as the breath attack turned into an ice pillar where they had been standing.

“Things are getting tough…”

If they kept avoiding attacks, the area would be filled with ice pillars, making it impossible to dodge. They might even become ice pillars themselves.

“Ichita-sama!”

“I understand!”

They entrusted the defeat to Ichita, who could attack from a distance. Ichita immediately aimed his new magic gun at the Ice Dragon and pulled the trigger. The Ice Dragon, sensing the incoming attack, fired a breath attack at Ichita.

Boom!

“You did it! As expected of Ichita-sama!”

“We won!”

Ichita’s attack clashed with the Ice Dragon’s, overwhelming it without resistance. The attack struck the Ice Dragon, charring it black. The dragon fell forward off the cliff, shattering on impact and turning into particles before vanishing. It left behind a treasure chest.

“What’s this…?”

“Scales.”

“Oh, they’re beautiful!”

Opening the treasure chest, they found several large, flat, transparent items. Ichita wasn’t sure what they were, but Satyrbell identified them as scales, likely from the Ice Dragon. Most drops were related to the defeated monster, so these glass-like, transparent items were probably Ice Dragon scales.

Velvet held up the Ice Dragon scales and changed the angle, watching as they refracted light into various colors—red, blue and a spectrum of seven colors. Velvet was captivated, comparing them to precious gems.

“Wow, these are tough. No wonder they’re Dragon scales.”

“They could make good shields.”

“With some work, they could be used for spearheads or daggers.”

They tapped the scales, noting their incredible strength. Such strength could be used to create protective shields or short-bladed weapons like spears or daggers.

“Galindo would be thrilled with these.”

“Definitely.”

They easily imagined that Galindo would be delighted to create something with the precious materials and they all laughed together.

“Alright, let’s move on to the next one.”

“Let’s go!”

“Kyu!”

After storing the drops using the Storage skill, they descended the staircase deeper into the area to advance.

“Huh… the sea…?”

“It’s all water.”

“Hmm… salty!”

When Ichita reached the fourth underground floor, they were greeted by a vast, blue expanse. It was so vast that it could be mistaken for the sea. Irithelis tasted the water and found it salty, indicating that this layer was designed to resemble the sea.

“…This is strange.”

“Yeah.”

Satyrbell and the others found the situation suspicious. They had been in the fourth layer for a while, but there was still no sign of monsters. Previously, monsters would attack as soon as they arrived, but now there were none. This unsettling atmosphere made it impossible not to be on guard.

“Look! Over there!”

“The sea surface!”

“Something’s coming!”

Suddenly, bubbles started to form in large quantities on the distant sea surface. They realized that something was rising and heightened their guard.

“W-what is that… it’s huge!”

“This is a massive creature…”

The area covered by bubbles kept expanding, leading them to expect an incredibly large monster. They became anxious, as large monsters were often strong and this one might be as powerful as the Ice Dragon.

“Ah… aaah!”

“Whoa!”

“What is that!”

Splash!

With a massive sound, something emerged from the sea onto the ground. Amidst the splashing water, Ichita and the others were shocked by the revealed form.

“Huge!”

Ichita was stunned by the enormous size. It was so large that it seemed closer than it actually was, distorting their sense of distance. It was several times larger than Serotiate, who had transformed into a dragon. If they included the part still in the sea, it would be even bigger.

Apart from Ichita, there were others who were greatly shocked. These were Irithelis and the others. It seemed they recognized the identity of the monster that had emerged from the sea. That’s why they were staring at the monster in disbelief. Even Serotiate, upon seeing the monster, was sweating profusely.

“L… L… L… Leviathan!”

Satyrbell shouted loudly at the gigantic monster that had appeared from the sea, conveying just how dangerous and perilous the situation was.

+++

## 250

“Leviathan… is this…”

Leviathan. A monstrous, gigantic creature with a serpent-like head and neck, a whale-like massive torso, an alligator-like hide and dragon-like wings and tail.

It often appears in games as one of the strongest creatures. Seeing it before him, Ichita is slightly moved and stunned by its immense size. Even from afar, it’s hard to grasp the full extent of the Leviathan.

“This is bad…”

“Overwhelmingly disadvantageous…”

“Damn it…”

Satyrbell and the others, realizing the Leviathan is their opponent, are bitterly frustrated, seemingly understanding how strong the enemy is.

“Worst case… Leviathan is said to be the strongest of all monsters…”

“A monster that far surpasses even dragons…!”

The Leviathan is a legendary creature with many tales, known to almost all aspiring adventurers. With its massive body and overwhelming strength, it is said to have faced multiple dragons. Its catastrophic strength was said to be capable of wiping out humanity, so it was buried by the gods.

“Hey… Seti… is this tale true…?”

“…Yes, it is a fact.”

The tale was true, as confirmed by Serotiate, who serves the gods and has lived longer than them. Stories can often be misinterpreted as they are passed down, but Serotiate, who witnessed the entire event of the Leviathan being buried by the gods, assured that it was true. Having seen it with her own eyes, she could not lie about the Leviathan’s strength and terror.

“Damn it… something like that is in the dungeon…!”

Everyone agreed, cursing the absurdity of a god-feared existence appearing in a dungeon.

Gyaaaaaaaaaaaaaaaaa!

“W-what!?”

“Ah…!”

“What the…!”

Suddenly, the Leviathan roared and bubbles began to erupt around it, revealing a multitude of powerful monsters like sea serpents, lemoras, kraken and hippocampi. The group was shocked and despairing, realizing they had to face not only the legendary Leviathan but also these formidable creatures.

Grrraaaaaaaaaaaaaaaaa!

“Seti!?”

“Y-yes!! There’s no time to despair!!”

To break the situation, Serotiate dragonized and unleashed her power. Seeing this, Satyrbell and the others also prepared for battle, determined not to be defeated.

Booooooooooom!!!!

“I-Ichita-sama!?”

“Hm? What is it?”

While everyone else was in despair, Ichita remained calm, continuing to take down monsters with his magic bullets as usual. Even facing the Leviathan, Ichita did not feel particular fear, though he acknowledged its size.

Satyrbell and the others, who had been tense and despairing, felt a bit relieved seeing Ichita’s usual demeanor.

“Let’s end this quickly before it gets messy!”

Booooooooooooom!!!!

Ichita wielded an old magic bullet gun in his left hand and a new one in his right, using dual wielding to hunt down a large number of monsters.

“I can’t fall behind!”

“Grraaaaaaaaaaa!”

“Good job, Tyr! Keep it up!”

“Hang in there!”

“Kyu!”

“Spilling over!”

“Leave it to me!”

“Here it goes!”

Satyrbell, skilled in magic and Serotiate, who casts magic from his mouth, followed Ichita. Although Velvet is also skilled in magic, she cannot use magic as powerful as Satyrbell’s. Instead, she and the others, who are mainly close combatants and not proficient in ranged attacks, cheered and watched over them.

Monsters that slipped through the attacks and approached Ichita and Satyrbell were immediately dealt with by Lilylea and the others. They could handle any that got close. Everyone focused on what they could do.

“…All right, it’s cleaned up. Now… it’s just you left!”

“Kyaaaaaaaaa!”

Booooooooooom!!!!

With most of the summoned monsters taken care of, Ichita aimed his gun at the source and fired. In response, the Leviathan opened its mouth and released a beam-like magic attack.

Ichita’s attack and the Leviathan’s attack collided, causing an explosion. An immense shockwave struck the surroundings and the sea churned violently.

“W-what…? An even match…!”

“N-no way!”

“First time seeing this!!”

Lilylea and the others were shocked that Ichita’s attack had failed for the first time. Until now, whenever Ichita attacked, monsters were always defeated in one hit. The realization that his attack had been countered was astonishing and they couldn’t hide their surprise. They once again acknowledged the Leviathan as a legendary creature.

“Impressive. Then how about this?”

Booooooooooooom!!!!

“Kyaaaaaaaaaaaaaaa!”

After one attack was countered, Ichita continued to fire in rapid succession. The Leviathan tried to counter, but the sheer volume of attacks made it difficult to counter them all and it took damage. Still, it fought back, spreading its wings and deploying numerous magic circles, from which it fired beam-like magic attacks.

“Careful!”

“Gaaaaaaaaaaaa!”

Ichita quickly countered all the attacks with his magic bullet gun. Serotiate managed to counter some, but since each counter was evenly matched, handling multiple attacks would be challenging.

“This isn’t working… Tyr! Does the Leviathan have any weaknesses?”

“W-weaknesses… I don’t know, but there’s a tale that it was defeated by holy magic!”

Ichita asked about the most effective method against the Leviathan. He was informed that the Leviathan was defeated by holy magic of the gods.

“Knowing that is enough!”

Ichita set a holy magic crystal on the revolver of his new magic bullet gun and adjusted the power lever to maximum.

“With this, I’ll finish it… uh oh!!!”

“Kyaaaaaaaaaaaaaaaaaa!”

As Ichita pulled the trigger, a massive holy magic beam bullet of unprecedented power was fired at the Leviathan. The recoil was so strong that Ichita’s body nearly bent backward.

Sensing danger, the Leviathan unleashed all its attacks toward Ichita’s magic bullet gun.

“Gooooooo (Kyuuuuuuu)!!!”

Ichita’s attack and the Leviathan’s attack clashed and after a brief standoff, Ichita’s attack absorbed the Leviathan’s. It then continued toward the Leviathan.

Booooooooooooom!!!!

Ichita’s most powerful attack hit its mark. As the smoke cleared, the Leviathan’s long neck and head were blown off. Without its head, the Leviathan’s body crumbled and sank into the sea.

“Did it!”

“As expected of Ichita-sama!”

“Amazing!”

“That legendary creature…!”

“I am in awe, sir!”

The group was amazed, excited and in awe that Ichita had defeated the legendary Leviathan. Ichita himself was relieved that he had emerged unscathed from the battle against the strongest monster he had ever faced.

“W-what…? H-huh!?”

“The cliff behind us…!”

Suddenly, a loud rumbling sound echoed and the cliff behind them began to crumble. The sea also started to churn violently, indicating that something unusual was happening in the dungeon.

“Could it be… the dungeon is collapsing!?”

“W-what!? Can that even happen!?”

“I don’t know!! This has never happened before!”

Everyone was confused and panicked, as they had never heard of or experienced such a phenomenon. The unknown situation left them unable to make any decisions and they were on the verge of chaos.

“Calm down, Tyr.”

“I-Ichita-sama…”

Ichita embraced the panicked Satyrbell and spoke softly to her, helping her regain her composure. He knew that panicking would only impair their judgment.

“…Thank you, Ichita-sama. I’m okay now.”

With Ichita’s kindness and reassurance, Satyrbell returned to her usual calm self and the group felt relieved.

“Everyone, gather around me! I’ll use magic to escape!”

“Finally!”

“Please do!”

“We count on you!”

“Kyuuuuu!”

Immediately, they took action to get through this situation. Satyrbell prepared to use a teleportation spell to escape the dungeon. Everyone else, eager to leave the area, quickly gathered around her.

“Ah!”

“What? We’re leaving now!”

“There’s a treasure chest over there…”

Irithelis spotted a treasure chest floating on the sea surface where the Leviathan had fallen. However, the teleportation spell was already activated, leaving no time to retrieve it. Moreover, preserving their lives was more important than the treasure, so Irithelis was persuaded to abandon the attempt to get the chest.

Thus, Ichita and the others used the teleportation magic to escape the collapsing dungeon.

+++

## 251

“Phew… we made it.”

Ichita and the others had safely escaped the collapsing dungeon, teleporting to the dungeon’s entrance and watching as it crumbled.

“It’s completely collapsed…”

“What happens now?”

“This is unprecedented… but since the dungeon has collapsed, maybe we’ve prevented a stampede… huh?”

They thought that with the entrance blocked, monsters would no longer be able to enter or exit, thus preventing a stampede.

The entrance was buried under rubble and the dungeon completely collapsed, causing the entrance to disappear in a burst of particles. Everyone was confused, wondering what had happened.

“The dungeon… is gone.”

“What’s going on…”

“Too many unknowns…”

Seeing the dungeon vanish, Ichita and the others were bewildered and gave up trying to understand. They decided to accept it as is, thinking that no matter how much they pondered, they wouldn’t find an answer.

“…So, what do we do now?”

“What?”

“Should we report it? About the dungeon?”

There is an obligation to report any newly discovered dungeons to the guild, as it serves various purposes such as avoiding danger and entertainment. That’s why they were discussing what to do.

“It might be better not to report it. It’s already gone.”

“True.”

They decided there was no need to report it. The dungeon had vanished and no one would believe them if they claimed it existed when it didn’t. They might be labeled as liars or eccentric. Therefore, they agreed to keep the existence of the dungeon a secret between themselves.

“All right, since the cause is resolved, let’s go home.”

“Sounds good. I’m tired.”

“Quite an eventful day.”

“I’m hungry~!”

“Kyuu!”

With the stampede resolved and no further reason to stay, they prepared to return home using Satyrbell’s teleportation magic.

“W-what!? Sir!”

“Huh!?”

“What!?”

“Y-you… bow and arrow!?”

Just then, an arrow flew toward Ichita. Serotiate managed to catch it at the last moment, preventing it from hitting Ichita.

Everyone except Serotiate was taken aback by the sudden event. They hadn’t sensed any presence, which was why they hadn’t reacted to the arrow. The fact that they were in an empty underground area made it even more surprising.

Ichita and the others quickly ran up the stairs and exited the underground area.

“…There’s no one here.”

“Right…”

“What’s going on…”

They looked around the surface but couldn’t find anyone. They thought someone might be hiding in the shadows, but since they couldn’t sense any human presence, they dismissed that idea.

They pondered who had attacked them and for what purpose, remaining vigilant as they scanned the area.

“Again!”

“Over there!”

Ichita was targeted by a bow again, but this time, Kikianhart was alert and sliced the arrow with her sword. They identified the direction from which the arrow had come, but there was no one there. However, as they focused their gaze, they saw a figure approaching from that direction.

“What were you doing here?”

“That’s our question for you.”

“Attacking us with a bow without warning!”

Appearing before Ichita and the others was a woman holding a bow, stopping about 10 meters away.

She had a strikingly beautiful face with double-lidded, sharp, upturned eyes and intense heterochromatic eyes. Her straight hair reached her chest, parted in the center, with a deep red color like wine. Her skin was the same brown as Velvet’s and she had a chest as large as Mireconia’s. She wore a tight black one-piece dress with intricate embroidery and deep slits on both sides from the waist down. She adorned herself with earrings and a necklace and her bracers and greaves were beautifully decorated in platinum. She also had a quiver slung diagonally across her back, holding arrows.

Among her features, what particularly caught their attention was…

“Y-you…”

“Could you be… an elf…?”

Satyrbell noticed that the woman shared a distinctive feature with herself — long ears. However, since she had never seen a brown-skinned elf before, she asked to confirm.

“…Yes and no.”

“What do you mean…?”

The woman responded with an ambiguous answer, so Satyrbell pressed for clarification.

“I am a child of a demon.”

“…Huh?”

“What are you talking about?”

They were genuinely confused, wondering what qualified her to call herself a ‘child of a demon’.

“Hmph. I don’t care about myself. Why are you here? This place is just a ruin now.”

“If that’s the case, we can ask you the same thing. Why are you here? There’s nothing here, you know?”

“…Because the mana was fluctuating.”

“Mana?”

They asked about her reason for coming to this place, wondering why she would come to a location known to be a pile of ruins and a finished site. However, since they were both asking the same question, the brown-skinned woman answered first.

“The mana in this area recently stabilized. The air, which had been unstable and murky, suddenly cleared. I was curious about why it cleared, so I came to investigate and found you here. What did you do?”

## Reborn In A World of Chastity Reversal - 135 - **The Night of That Day (3) ~BOYS BE AMBITIOUS~**

Many of them did so probably because they had club activities the next morning and wanted to avoid the hassle of traveling to and from their homes. There were also some students who did so because they wanted to spend the night with their friends, affected by the festive mood.

Naturally, among them, there were also boys and girls who were in romantic relationships.

Leaving two rooms empty in between, it seemed that the third-year girls would stay in rooms 406 and onwards on the same fourth floor, and the other girls would stay in the rooms beyond all the way to the second floor in order of their grade.

There were no other first-year boys staying overnight there, only second- and third-years, so Yuu was told that he would be sharing a room with second-year boys.

There wasn’t much interaction between the boys who were in different grades, so he only knew a few of them, but he should be able to manage somehow. In fact, he thought about using this opportunity to broaden his circle of friends.

He thought so, but Yuu found himself in an unexpected situation.

As soon as he went up to the fourth floor and got near room 403, he was called out by a third-year student who had gone out to the hallway.

As he was, he was taken to room 401 and was immediately surrounded by a large group of people.

There were more than ten second- and third-year students in the eight-person room, so it felt cramped.

At first, he wondered if they were intending to put him, a cheeky first-year student, in his place… or, even if it wasn’t to such an extent, to give him harsh but honest advice as seniors.

The ace of the Kendo club Hayase Mika and singer Ishima Mariko. He was an exceedingly handsome guy who was dating two contrasting but both very attractive third-year girls.

He got acquainted with him when they cheered together at the Kendo club tournament in May.

He had also met and exchanged greetings with him in the rear garden a number of times when he went to the student council, so he didn’t think he disliked him.

## 148 - **At Sairei Academy (1) ~Melody~**

Private Sairei Academy High School was located in the north-western part of Sakate City, adjacent to the south of Saiou City.

It was far from the station and urban areas, and as could be seen from the fact that Saitama Natural Zoological Park, which Sairyou Academy used for its new students orienteering event, was nearby, the surrounding area was full of greenery.

From Sairyou Academy, it was less than 20 minutes by car, or about 30 minutes by bicycle.

If you were to look at the grounds of Sairei Academy from above, you would be able to see that the four buildings formed a slightly elongated rectangular shape.

The school building located on the top side, which happened to be on the north side, was Building A, which was used by the general education department.

The buildings on the left and right (east and west) were Buildings B and C, which were used by the art departments.

The school building located on the bottom side (south) and mainly used by teachers – what other schools would call the administration building – was Building D. Each school building was three stories high, and the second floor of each building was connected by a passageway.

The main gate was located on the south side of the school grounds, and a long road stretched straight to the entrance in the center of Building D.

On the east side of the road was a large parking lot that could accommodate about 150 cars. Across the road on the west side was a multi-purpose hall with a height comparable to a three-storey school building.

To the north of Building A stood all sorts of sports facilities, such as two grounds, one large and one small, tennis courts, a gymnasium, indoor practice areas, and even a swimming pool.

Its scale surpassed that of Sairyou Academy which was in the neighboring city.

To begin with, Sairei Academy was founded 20 years ago.

Half of the students were enrolled in arts-specialized departments, which were rare for high schools, and the other half in general education departments, but their goal was to attract and nurture talented people who excelled in both academics and sports.

That plan was only half successful.

Due to their excellent facilities and instructors that were assembled using the money and connections of the Ayakuni Group, they were able to take part in national competitions and exhibitions in just a few years, and they had even produced a number of graduates who went on to art and music universities and made a name for themselves as professionals.

On the other hand, the general education department had been having a hard time attracting students.

There was a reason for this.

When it came to academics and sports, their sister school, Sairyou Academy, in the neighboring city was widely known.

In the first place, even among the board of directors, there were dissenting opinions on them taking the trouble of building a school in the neighboring city of Sairyou Academy.

However, there was this adult circumstance in which as they planned to open a university campus in the same city, they had finished the acquisition process, but the plan was suddenly canceled, so the Ayakuni Group, which was looking for a suitable site for a new school, decided to choose this place.

If this had been in the southern part of the prefecture, where the population was high, it might not have been that much of a problem, but in the central part of the prefecture, where there were only a few large cities, the capacity of the neighboring area was too small.

As feared, the general education department continued to fail to reach its full capacity for some time, and even among those who enrolled, many were low-level students who failed to get into nearby public high schools.

Athletic club activities were also slow, and the extensive sports facilities, which they had taken the trouble of building, ended up turning into pearls throws before swine.

While art-related students were achieving excellent results and raising the reputation of Sairei Academy, they were dragged down by general education students who liked to cause troubles; such a trend continued for some time.

For this reason, when the Ayakuni Group decided to make one of the schools under them coeducational 15 years ago, the Sairei side touted mainly its new and excellent facilities, but the biggest obstacle was undoubtedly the quality of its students.

After it was decided that they would make Sairyou coeducational, the sister school social event that had been regularly held until then with Sairei, which lost to them, was terminated, and the rift between the two schools ended up deepening.

However, that was when Sairei’s reforms began.

First, they drastically reduced the enrollment capacity of the general education department, which had a deviation score of less than 40, from 130 to 90 per grade (in exchange, they slightly increased the enrollment capacity of art-related departments).

Then, they established a college preparatory course.

A special college preparatory course for students who aimed to go on to famous universities (depending on their grades, they might have their entrance fee, or even their tuition fees waived).

And also a management preparatory course for students who wanted to learn about society from a broad perspective and become entrepreneurs or managers.

And then, in order to bring the remaining students in the regular courses up to average level, they also strove to improve the quality of the teachers.

It was also around this time that – in order to allow the students to discipline the students of the general education department, who tended to be unruly, themselves – the power of the student council was strengthened.

For a while after the school’s founding, the student council officers were made up of students from various art departments, but after two or three years, students from the special college preparatory course and management preparatory course began to join them.

Eventually, in the final section, the piece reached its climax with the raging force of all the instruments.

For that reason, when the piece reached its climax, Yuu’s heart was overcome with emotion, and the moment the performance was over, he reflexively stood up and gave a huge round of applause.

It was said that music transcended national borders.

Perhaps it meant that even those who were at odds with each other due to different religions, ethnic groups or economic backgrounds could become one under the charm of music.

Although they had opened up a little after they settled for a draw in the quiz championship held some time ago, Yuu and the other Sairyou students’ impression of Sairei was not that good.

However, in the face of their excellent performance, the lingering ill feelings vanished, and they were left with a feeling of honest admiration for them.

Seeing that the third-year students were still waiting for their turn, it looked like the first-years wouldn’t be able to get in any time soon, so Yuu excused himself to his friend and approached Kate.

Perhaps she had gone to the girls’ bathroom, the other girl from the student council wasn’t by her side, so it was good timing.

「Good work.」

「Ah, you… that’s not good. For you to be here by yourself….」

「Isn’t it fine? I’m only here to hello to someone I know, after all.」

「Geez.」

Kate sighed at Yuu’s behavior.

As far as Yuu was concerned, even he had only done it because he judged that in the current situation, where there was a group of Sairyou students nearby, it should be fine.

There were security guards standing at the entrance to stop unrelated Sairei students from entering, and the Sairiei’s female students who had watched the performance hadn’t come to the entrance, perhaps out of consideration for them.

「The recital was much better than I expected. Everyone was moved.」

When Yuu praised them, even Kate, who usually had a cool expression on her face, broke into a smile.

「That’s good to hear. I heard that the people who were chosen to perform today had spent all their time practicing as if they were possessed, not taking even a single day off, even after entering summer vacation, after all.」

「Ooh. If that’s the case, it was all the more worthwhile coming.」

「I’m sure they’re also happy that you came.」

The conversation stopped there, and silence prevailed for a while.

Kate, who looked down a little, glanced at Yuu and was about to speak.

Sensing her gaze, Yuu showed a puzzled look on his face.

After hesitating for a moment, Kate muttered without making eye contact with him.

「Say, after this…」

「Huh?」

In part due to the hustle and bustle from the surrounding area, her small voice was hard to hear.

「About this afternoon…」

「Afternoon? Ah, you mean the student council matter?」

「Yes…」

However, before he could hear the rest of what she wanted to say, they heard someone calling out to Yuu.

It seemed like their turn to use the bathroom had come.

「I’ll get going then.」

「Wait.」

Kate hurriedly took out her student handbook and pen, scribbled something on it, then tore off a page with her hand.

Then she leaned over to Yuu and handed it to him, hiding it from the prying eyes of those around them.

「Go into the bathroom and read it. When you’re done, tear it up and flush it down.」

「Huh?」

「Just do it, hurry up!」

「O… ooh.」

After that, Yuu, who went to the bathroom with a number of first-year boys, deliberately went into a toilet stall.

There, he unfolded the piece of paper Kate had given him.

The following was written on it.

『The student council members are up to something. Quickly go home before they do something to you. 』

◇ ◇ ◇

「Is something the matter, Yuu?」

「Huh?」

「Well, you’ve been spacing out for a while now, so…」

「Yuu-kun, is there something you’re worried about?」

「Err… It, it’s nothing!」

「In that case, good, but…」
