Despite the fact that it was summer vacation, for today, it seemed like the staff had prepared meals for them.

Though, perhaps because it was a provisional operation, there were only three options available today: Set Meal A, which was mainly meat; Set Meal B, which was fish; and Set Meal C, which was a lighter set consisting of pasta, soup, and salad.

Yuu, who chose set A, Masaya, who chose set B, and Rei, who chose set C, sat around a table, but Yuu’s chopsticks were unmoving because he was bothered by what was written on the piece of paper he had been given earlier.

The thing that Riko told him yesterday flashed through his mind.

Which was, in exchange for not laying their hands on ordinary male students, they, with Sairei’s student council president Mitsuse Rinne and vice president Oomori Norika in the lead, were probably planning to approach Yuu.

Looking at their past history, he could easily imagine that.

Not to mention that Sayaka had been in poor health for a while now.

They would still say hello at least, but if they kept pestering him, it would probably be best to refuse it firmly and then put an end to the meeting as soon as possible.

Having made up his mind, Yuu nodded his head to the two, who had a worried look on their faces, to reassure them, and then started eating.

The meal that was served was very delicious considering the low price for students, and they ate it up in no time at all.

◇ ◇ ◇

For a while after the meal, the Sairyou students chatted together, not separately into boys and girls’ groups, but it seemed like the time had come.

The students who served as their guide began to stand by the wall with placards.

The afternoon session would take place in building B and C, and the main focus was on taking a look at the exhibitions by the various art departments and thriving cultural clubs.

There were music department-concert band club-chorus club course, arts-crafts department-related club course, calligraphy and Japanese performing arts-related club course, and drama and light music club course.

It was scheduled to start at 1:30pm and end at 4:30pm.

Setting aside the girls, even the boys got bored halfway through it, they couldn’t just let them go home arbitrarily. In such a case, the arrangement was to ask them to go back to the bus and wait.

For better or worse, the cafeteria was open to Sairyou students and was designated as a rest area (Sairei students were not allowed to enter except the ones serving as guides).

Apparently, the cooking club would be treating them to homemade cookies from 3pm.

It truly felt like they were being taken care of thoroughly.

Masaya, of course, wanted to take the music department-concert band club-chorus club course.

Rei, who had always been fond of tea ceremony, flower arrangement, and calligraphy and was interested in traditional Japanese performing arts, seemed to want to take the calligraphy and Japanese performing arts-related club course.

They would also be going separately from Yuu, who planned to visit the student council with Sayaka and the others.

The boys, who split according to the courses they wanted to take, would be accompanied by five times as many girls and security guards, so Yuu thought, 「I guess there’s nothing to worry about.」, and said goodbye to the two for a while.

As he walked towards Sayaka, Riko, and Emi, who were waiting for him near the entrance to the school cafeteria, Yuu recalled the note Kate had given him earlier.

Just in case, he thought it would probably be best to tell the three of them.

However, the moment Yuu got close to them, he was taken by the hand and led to a corner.

「What’s the matter?」

「Um, err, you see…」

「Sayaka.」 「Saaya-senpai!」

「Ah, yes.」

It seemed like Sayaka had something to say.

Urged by the two, Sayaka looked straight at Yuu from the front.

Her expression was very serious.

「Yuu-kun」

「Yes.」

「You’ll go back to school on your way home today, right?」

Yuu nodded.

The plan was to disperse after returning to school.

「I’m sorry, but could you stop by the student council room before you go home?」

「Hmm? I don’t really mind, but…」

The cheering for the clubs had just come to an end for the time being, so once today’s business was over, there shouldn’t be any urgent business for the student council.

Sayaka exchanged looks with Riko and Emi, then nodded.

「A, actually, all three of us have something important to tell you, Yuu-kun.」

「And that’s… something you want to talk about with just the four of us after we’re done here, not right now, right?」

「Y, yes.」

Since Sayaka and the others said it was an important matter, the option of refusing didn’t exist within Yuu.

「Got it. Sure thing. See you on our way home then.」

Hearing Yuu’s reply, Sayaka and the others showed a relieved smile.

「Well then, let’s get the bothersome stuff out of the way quickly, shall we?」

「Yes. After putting an end to it early, we can also join the tour group. Yuu-kun, do you want to take a look at it together?」

「I suppose so. If Sayaka is feeling well, I’d like to take a look at it with the four of us.」

「Yes. It seems like Sairei’s side is being more considerate than I thought, but I want to see it for myself.」

As they were discussing their next course of action, the matter about the memo he had been given earlier ended up getting pushed into the corner of Yuu’s mind.

The four of them left the cafeteria and went out to the courtyard.

Unlike inside the school buildings, which were cool and air-conditioned, they were immediately hit by the strong summer sun, and sweat seemed to start to pour out of them.

In the courtyard, there was a fountain in the center where the promenades connecting the various school buildings crossed, benches were placed here and there, and colorful flowers were blooming in the flower beds.

As expected, in addition to the fact that it was summer vacation, their students were scattered to accommodate the Sairyou students who were visiting the school, so there were no students to be seen.

They could imagine it being a place for students to relax during breaks and after school.

They had been told that the three-story building that stood tall like a tower in the lawn that spread southeast from the fountain plaza was the student council building.

When they stepped through the door on the north side and into the entrance, they found that it was cool inside.

It seemed that the whole building here was air-conditioned too, talk about luxurious.

She must have recognized Yuu and the others as they entered.

A girl at the reception booth greeted them with a smile and started to contact someone on the phone.

「Huh? They’re already here. But… Well… yes. I, I see…」

「Is something the matter?」

「Fweh?!」

Calling out to the girl, who was confused, was Yuu.

Perhaps never expected to be spoken to by a boy out of the blue, she was so flustered that she dropped the phone she was about to put down.

「Ah, sorry. I believe we are right on time as mentioned in the invitation, though?」

「No… It seems that there are some confusions about the preparations upstairs. If you could just wait a moment…」

「Preparation? Since we have come all the way here, we are thinking of saying hello at least, but we plan to go home without staying too long here today, you see. I’m sorry to trouble you, but can you call them for me?」

「No, um… If you don’t want to wait, that would put us in trouble, though.」

「Can’t you at least call the student council members?」

「Err, that…」

「Oh my?」

Just as they were about to start arguing, a woman who happened to come down the stairs noticed Yuu and the others and called out to them.

「Are you the Sairyou student council, by any chance? Welcome.」

「Ah, hello.」

「「「Hello!」」」

The woman, who was going through middle age weight gain, dressed in gray pants and a white blouse was probably in her late 40 or around 50.

She had the air of a somewhat pushy teacher, moreover one who held a certain status.

She was probably the vice principal or head of the grade.

「Our student council is waiting for you. Do come in.」

「No, I’m sorry for all the efforts you have put into it, but we only want to say hello….」

The receptionist girl told them to wait, and the teacher in front of them told them to go in.

As far as Yuu and the others were concerned, they wanted to just say hello here, but…

「It’s the prided student council office of generations of student council presidents, you see. It’s definitely worth a look. You’ve come all the way here, so you should just quickly go in and make yourself at home. Come on now!」

This kind of aunty was the type of person who wouldn’t listen to what people said and just pushed you along.

Even so, she believed that she was doing a good thing, so you would have a hard time dealing with her.

Yuu and the others were hesitant, but when the teacher pointed to the stairs with a hand gesture, saying 「go ahead, go ahead」, it was hard to refuse.

As expected, it seemed that she showed some reservation when it came to Yuu, but she went behind Sayaka and the others and kept pushing them towards the stairs.

Sayaka and the others, who had indescribable expressions on their faces, and Yuu headed for the stairs as the teacher saw them off.

「It seems like not only the third floor; the other floors are reserved for the student council as well.」

「This whole building is reserved for the student council, huh. To think there’s even a dedicated conference room.」

「They have a huge budget for the student council, you see.」

「Even though we’re both private schools, there’s a huge difference there, isn’t there~?」

The Sairyou student council office was simple and unadorned, as it was located inside the boarding house.

Moreover, it had been more than 30 years since it was built, so age-related deterioration was noticeable here and there.

However, perhaps it had been renovated once, this building in which the Sairei student council was located had a new interior, and it gave off the impression of a stylish office in the city.

As they climbed the stairs and reached the third floor, they suddenly heard a stern voice coming from inside.

「You haven’t finished the preparations yet?! Even though they’re already here.」

「There seems to have been some kind of mistake… I’m going to get it now!」

「Good graciousness! If there’s something wrong with the arrangements, I’ll hold you responsible!」

「I, I’m terribly sorry.」

「It’s kind of hectic over there.」

「Yeah.」

「Shall we come in?」

He knocked, but there was no response.

As before, all they could hear were swearing and constant apologies.

Judging from the familiar sounding voice, it seemed that it was the student council president who was mainly doing the swearing.

He felt disinclined to go in there, but they couldn’t just wait there forever.

Sayaka and Riko had an exasperated look on their faces. Eimi was scared and stuck close to Yuu’s back.

He already felt like going home, but he was scared of what might happen afterwards, so he had no choice but to open the door quietly.

「Hello~」

「「「Ah!」」」

Although Yuu had never been in such a place throughout his life prior to his rebirth, the spacious, stately, and chic interior reminded him of the director offices of large companies he saw on TV.

Facing the window on the right side as you entered, the tables were arranged in a U-shape, but just by looking at it, they seemed to be made of authentic office materials, unlike the Sairyou student council office.

On the left side was a black leather lounge suit, and on the one-person sofa directly in front of Yuu as he entered, the president was leaning back as she sat with her legs crossed.

As such, Yuu’s eyes ended up getting drawn to her long bare legs, which were exposed right up to her thighs.

Upon noticing Yuu, Rinne hurriedly stood up, tidied up her long hair, brushed her one-piece uniform to smooth out the wrinkles, and plastered a graceful smile on her face.

「Oh my! Thank you for coming! We have ordered some rare, high-quality tea leaves from overseas for this day. But unfortunately, the tea isn’t ready yet…」

「No, please don’t worry about it. As we are planning to go home as soon as we have said hello to you.」

「I, I’m sorry. For being late… Ah!」

「Kyaa!」

「Hmm?」

When Yuu turned around at the sound of the voice, he saw someone who had come into the room in a hurried manner and was about to bump into Eimi, who was near the entrance.

Perhaps their posture as they tried to forcefully avoid her was poor, the person, who was shorter than Eimi, stumbled and nearly fell forward.

「Whoa!」

「Oops.」

Yuu took a step forward and caught the brown paper bag flying at him with his chest and grabbed it with his left hand.

At the same time, he caught the small figure, who had let go of the bag and was about to fall toward him with their arms outstretched, and supported them with his right hand.

With short, curly black hair, and dressed in a white shirt and black shorts, that person looked like a boy younger than Yuu.

「Hu… h…?」

「Are you okay?」

When the boy looked up, Yuu could see that he had dark skin and chiseled features, perhaps he was from West Asia.

He stared at Yuu with his wide-open, black eyes.

「I, I’m sorry.」

「Amir!」

「Ha!」

「That’s rude to our guests!」

「For you to be such a dullard at such a crucial moment.」

「Did you get caught by another woman and come?」

Perhaps Amir was his name.

The one who scolded him in a harsh tone was Rinne.

Yuu didn’t notice right away, but it seemed that Vice President Li Weifei and Oomori Norika were standing with their arms folded by the wall at the far-left side of the room.

As far as Yuu was concerned, he found the scene before his eyes unsettling.

That was because up until now, he had never seen a scene of a woman harshly scolding a man.

Not to mention that the boy in front of him was still young, looking to be around 12 or 13 years old.

He might even be an elementary school student.

However, Amir, who quickly got away from him, bowed deeply not only to Yuu but to everyone in the room.

「I, I’m terribly sorry. Right away…」

「If you have time to talk, just get on with it already!」

「Wait a moment. I don’t know what happened, but no matter how you look at it, he’s too pitiable, no?」

「Huh?」

He had no idea what kind of circumstances were at play here.

It was just that, Yuu felt sorry for Amir who was being treated so harshly by older women, or rather, he simply thought it was not right for people to group up and scold someone much younger than them, regardless of gender.

As Amir, who became teary-eyed, was about to walk away with his back hunched, Yuu held his shoulder and stepped forward to protect him.

「Yuu-kun…」

Sayaka and the others showed a worried look on their faces.

Rinne and the others showed a puzzled look on their faces, their eyes widened as if they found it really surprising.

「Y, you see, ever since his parents took refuge in Japan, I’ve been taking care of him and having him help out at the Sairei Student Council, so…」

「Even so, he’s still a child, isn’t he? It’s human natures to make mistakes, so you can just watch over him with warm eyes, no?」

「Well…」

As far as Yuu was concerned, he just wanted to say something about the way these girls, who were high school students and practically adults, treated Amir, who was still a child. There was no difference between men and women there.

Sayaka and the others also quickly stood next to Yuu to protect Amir, and the two sides began glaring at each other.

Seeing this, Rinne looked annoyed for a moment, but eventually sighed in resignation.

「Phew. I understand. I believed that to discipline a child of this age it was essential to treat them in a strict manner, but as opposed to just scolding them, I guess it’d be a good idea to watch over them gently from time to time. Now, Amir, prepare the tea for our guests.」

「Y, yes! Um… thank you very much!」

「You’re welcome.」

Yuu smiled at Amir, who bowed deeply in front of him.

But then he remembered. That they came here today with the intention of getting it over with quickly.

「Um, you see, about today…」

「Now, come over here.」

「Mitsuse-san!」

Yuu called out to Rinne’s back as she headed towards the door at the back without listening to what he said.

When Rinne turned around, she had a slightly dissatisfied look on her face.

「As I told you before, we should call each other by our first names.」

「Ah… that aside, I appreciate your kind invitation, but we’re thinking about going home after just saying hello to you….」

「Thanks to the excellent recital in the morning, our male students are looking forward to the tour in the afternoon, you see. As such, we would like to go around and take a look at that instead.」

「Maybe we can hold the review meeting for the quiz championship at another time?」

Following Yuu, Sayaka and Riko also added their words as if to provide cover.

Hearing this, the expression vanished from Rinne’s face, looking as if it had turned into a Noh mask.

「Oh dear. Amir, who you all protected earlier, is doing his best to prepare tea, you know? He’ll probably be disappointed if we let that go to waste.」

「Ugh…」

Yuu was also perplexed by Norika’s words as she stood next to Rinne.

She had a radiant smile on her face, but she was hitting on their weak spot.

He exchanged looks with Sayaka and the others on either side of him.

「Hmm… It might be impolite to leave without even having a cup of tea.」

「When you put it like that…」

「Well, it’s true that I’m a little thirsty.」

「Then, since they’ve taken the trouble to prepare some tea, why not?」

Nodding at each other, Yuu and the others decided to have just one cup of tea, and followed Rinne and the others into the back room.

+++

## 150 - **At Sairei Academy (3) ~Spinning the Roulette of Fate~**

They learned that Amir was born in a rural area near the Caspian Sea in a country that was once called Persia and was nowadays called Iran.

Amir had no memories of his hometown.

That was because as soon as he was born and found out to be a boy, his mother, who was born into a wealthy family and was the leader of a community that was at odds with the village chief, took Amir and left the village.

Ever since all the young men in the village died out a long time ago due to the outbreak of Red Death, and all the children that were born afterwards were girls, there had been a long-standing tradition of men being the common property of the village.

In the village with a population of about 200, there were only about 6 to 7 men at most.

Immediately after birth, boys were locked up in a sturdy stone manor built next to the village chief’s house.

This was to prevent them from being found and attacked or kidnapped by women from outside.

Although they received preferential treatment in meals, they were not allowed to go outside except to the small courtyard, and had few opportunities to move their bodies, so many of them bulked up and became fat while they were still children.

However, as soon as they had their first ejaculation, they were made to accompany the women of the village every night, so they ended up losing weight.

While some women remained full of energy even after reaching 60 or 70 years old, few men lived beyond 40 years old due to their debauched lifestyle.

Amir’s mother did not want her child, who had been born as a boy, to live such a life.

You could call it a mother’s ego.

She fervently hoped that she could allow him to live a life where he could choose his own way of life, even if it was not to the same extent as a woman.

Even though she had been living in the countryside, as she was from a wealthy family, she knew that there were some countries where men were given preferential treatment.

It was also fortunate that partly because she gave birth to him prematurely, her parents happened to be away in another village.

First, she confided her plan to only one woman – her attendant who was also her close friend and loyal servant – and obtained her cooperation.

After giving the only woman who knew it was a boy strong alcohol that day to keep her mouth shut, they took all the money they could carry out of the house and fled the village in a Japanese car, the best car in the village.

The mothers traveled to the capital via a nearby town, but unfortunately, a political upheaval occurred in the country and public safety was rapidly deteriorating.

As they had a baby with them, their plan to settle down in the capital for a while ended up getting off the rails.

In the situation where martial law might be imposed at any given moment, if the military women who were throwing their weight around in the city found out that the child was a boy, they might take him away.

Fortunately, they had plenty of money, so the group traveled a long distance south, refueling every now and then, to a large city on the Persian Gulf.

There, they gathered information and learned that a ship that sailed to Japan via Southeast Asia and Taiwan was going to set sail.

Thus, Amir’s mother spent the rest of their money and managed to leave the country, but the attendant, who had fallen ill after her first long voyage in her life, ended up getting bedridden.

As the person in question strongly asked her not to worry about her, they tearfully parted ways in Malaysia, and the mother and son entered Japan as refugees.

Three months had passed since they had left the village.

Partly because she had a baby boy with her, even though they were also refugees, they were given special preferential treatment, and their permission to live in Japan was granted right away, which was fortunate.

The mother had been on edge for a long time, but as soon as she realized that life in Japan was going to be manageable one way or another, the repercussions of pushing herself too hard after giving birth seemed to suddenly wash over her.

There were many times when she had to stay in bed for days, and because she had no experience with physical labor and the language barrier, she was unable to find work.

Thus, for about ten years, they lived a modest life in a government-run apartment in south-western part of Saitama Prefecture, relying on boy’s allowances and living assistance.

Even so, the mother was satisfied.

That was because, unlike in the village, mother and son could live together there.

The baby boy, named Amir, grew up well in Japan, where public safety was good.

When he learned that his mother had abandoned her hometown in which she was born and raised shortly after giving birth to him and forced herself to come all the way to Japan for him, he was filled with the desire to repay her for her kindness.

However, at his age, he was not able to work, and could only help with the household chores at best.

It happened when Amir was 11 years old and had just entered the sixth grade.

A cold-looking woman in a black suit spoke to Amir on his way home from school.

According to her, a certain rich young lady was looking for a boy to be her attendant.

All he had to do was take the men’s bus to the young lady’s school and serve her for two or three hours every day after school from Monday to Saturday, and he would be paid more than a highschool student would earn at a part-time job.

Amir jumped at the opportunity.

It was because he wanted to make his mother’s life easier, even if only a little.

In the student council office at Sairei Academy, to which Amir had been commuting since April, his main duties were to prepare refreshments and serve as a waiter, and in the beginning, because he was unfamiliar with the environment and work, he was at a loss what to do and was often scolded.

However, now he had become completely accustomed to it, and sometimes he even got praised.

Apart from that, it was a daily occurrence for him to have his body groped and teased as he served as the chatting partner for young lady Rinne’s group.

It had been known that he had already had his first ejaculation.

He was aware that the day when he had his virginity taken by the most powerful person in the student council, young lady Rinne, the president, or Norika, the vice-president, who had been sexually harassing him time and again since a long time ago, would probably come soon.

Even so, it’s fine; So Amir thought.

If he could be of more use, he would be paid more, right?

It seemed that when he, a boy, went on to middle school, it would cost much more money.

For his mother’s sake, it would be best if he could increase the money he earned.

On the summer day Amir had such a thought.

He met an older boy named Yuu.

◇ ◇ ◇

Since they entered summer vacation, it was decided that he would only serve them on the days when they had a student council meeting.

As there was a special event, he was told to come by 12 o’clock on August 3rd.

As soon as he arrived, Amir received a call on his extension phone.

It was a female voice he didn’t recognize, but it was a message from the student council president, telling him to go get a certain item stored in the storage room and do as the note inside said.

Without any suspicion, Amir headed to School Building A.

As it was during the summer vacation, building A, which was usually noisy with general education department students, was deserted, so there were no prying eyes, which was convenient for him.

That was because although no girls would probably bother Amir, who was wearing an armband with 『Student Council』 prominently written on it, he would like to avoid getting spotted and stared scrutinizingly at by female students.

The so-called storage room was the two rooms that the student council had used before moving to its current location.

One of the rooms was cramped and dusty, filled with cardboard boxes filled with tools used in past events and all kinds of old documents piled up here and there.

The room Amir entered was the one that used to be used for meetings.

He avoided the desks and chairs stacked in the middle and headed toward the steel shelves along the wall.

According to the instructions, the item was placed there in a conspicuous place.

But no matter how hard he searched, he could not find the item he was looking for.

Amir began to get anxious as time passed.

With the windows closed, the room was unusually hot and humid, and sweat was pouring down like crazy.

Even after searching every nook and cranny of the two steel shelves, he was unable to find it.

Maybe he should go back to the student council office and ask them to tell him the instructions again.

Even if he got scolded for it.

After searching for over an hour, being at a loss what to do a number of times, finally, as he turned towards the door, he kicked something.

For the love of all that was holy.

For one reason or another, he ended up dropping it as soon as he started searching around, but it was a light paper bag and didn’t make a sound, so he didn’t notice it.

The clock was already striking 1:30.

At any rate, Amir grabbed the small brown paper bag he was looking for and ran to the student council office.

The moment Amir ran up the stairs and entered the room through the open door, perhaps because he was in a hurry, he almost bumped into a girl in a uniform he didn’t know.

「I, I’m sorry. For being late… Ah!」

「Kyaa!」

Amir barely managed to avoid her, but lost his balance and ended up stumbling.

「Whoa!」

「Oops.」

For some reason, at that moment, he felt as if time was moving slowly.

He watched in dismay as the paper bag, which left his hands as he stumbled, flew into the air, but a boy who had turned around caught it with his chest and grabbed it firmly with his left hand at the same time.

He then immediately reached out his right hand, took Amir’s arm as he was about to fall forward, and pulled him towards him.

「Hu… h…?」

「Are you okay?」

Who on earth is this person?

He looks really cool and kind.

It was only for a brief moment that Amir entertained such a thought, as soon after, Rinne’s reprimand shot toward him.

The student council officers, including Rinne, were merciless towards Amir, who was still an elementary school student.
